Current Commentary

Illegal Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway and Relations Between Japan and Russia 21

— Ji

Negotiations between Japan and the Soviet Union regarding the illegal sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway began in June 1933. After countless twists and turns, both parties finally reached an agreement on January 22 of this year. The Russian side, not hesitating to accept a minimum price of 140 million yuan, ceded the railway to the Japanese. The official signing is scheduled for the 23rd of this month. Our government, regarding this matter as concerning sovereignty, naturally finds it difficult to remain silent. Therefore, it has repeatedly lodged protests with both the Soviet and Japanese sides. On the 16th of this month, another severe protest was lodged. At the same time, based on the Sino-Soviet Agreement of the 13th year of the Republic of China, statements were sent to all relevant countries, reiterating our country's position. Although its effect is currently difficult to foresee, it is an appropriate and necessary action to deny this illegal sale and preserve all our country's rights on the railway.

The Soviet Union's transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway within our country's borders not only disregards our country's sovereignty, but also violates the Sino-Soviet Agreement, an illegal and unreasonable action. Considering that Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations have already been restored today, we cannot help but feel deeply regretful. However, considering the reason why the Soviet Union disregarded China's interests and acted so recklessly, it is also related to the recent changes in the international environment. It is because (1) since Japan invaded and occupied the four northeastern provinces of our country and organized a puppet state, Japan and Russia have been in a position of direct conflict at all times, and the dispute over the Chinese Eastern Railway has a great possibility of becoming a fuse for war between the two countries. Now, the Russian side has to make many concessions to Japan to seek temporary peace, and its purpose is to勉强maintain peace in order to carry out its original plan for socialist construction. (2) Since the completion of the Jihui, Laha, Binbei, and other railways in the puppet Manchukuo, the Chinese Eastern Railway has long lost its independence in terms of economics. Even if war breaks out between Japan and Russia, the outcome will not depend on the gains or losses of this railway. (3) In terms of relations with Western Europe, Hitler's ambition is pressing. His attempt to seize Ukraine through Poland has never ceased for a single day. Recently, he openly declared the abolition of the military clauses in the Treaty of Versailles and is reorganizing his military. In particular, he dared to be a vanguard against the Soviet Union. The Soviet Union has long been aware of this situation. In order to avoid the danger of being attacked by both the East and the West, it had to make concessions to Japan on the Chinese Eastern Railway issue.

However, can the success of the illegal transfer negotiations of the Chinese Eastern Railway ease the tense relations between Japan and the Soviet Union? This is also an issue worthy of our attention. Commentators often say, "The success of the Chinese Eastern Railway transfer negotiations is not only enough to eliminate the Soviet Union's source of redification in the Far East, but also the diplomatic disputes between Japan and Russia can be swept away from now on. Therefore, after the establishment of the Chinese Eastern Railway sale, Japan's rule over Manchuria will become more consolidated, and the South Manchuria Railway can also let go of its operations on the entire Manchurian railway, making it easier to develop resources in northern Manchuria. Exports to Russia are gradually increasing. As a result, Japan-Soviet relations can become more and more缓和, and the diplomatic relations between the two countries may become more peaceful and friendly." However, according to our observations, the success of the Chinese Eastern Railway transfer between Japan and the Soviet Union is indeed a preliminary success in easing Japan-Soviet relations. However, if one is too optimistic about the future Japan-Soviet relations, I am afraid it is too early. Why? The center of gravity of Japan-Soviet relations is not entirely in the resolution of the Chinese Eastern Railway dispute, but in how the non-aggression treaty is concluded. Whether Japan is willing to sign a non-aggression treaty with Russia is an important key to whether the relations between the two countries can truly move towards缓和 in the future. How the international relations in East Asia will develop in the future will also change depending on the changes in this issue. Secondly, what we should pay attention to is the fishery conflict between Japan and the Soviet Union in the coastal area of ​​Vladivostok. The intention of the Japanese side is to eliminate the Soviet Union's fishery forces along the eastern coast. Whether the Russian side is willing to give in to this is a big question. Again, the ambition of the Japanese military is to seize the eastern coastal Primorsky Krai of Russian Siberia. At the same time, eliminate the potential forces of the Soviet Union in Outer Mongolia and Xinjiang to complete the necessary preparations for its exclusive occupation of East Asia. Now, although the transfer of the Chinese Eastern Railway has been successful, whether the Japanese side will stop at the right time and be willing to maintain a lasting peace with the Soviet Union, I am afraid that no one dares to make a positive prediction at present. If the Japanese side is not satisfied with this and makes further demands, will the Russian side continue to retreat step by step and not resist? This is also a question that is worth pondering and imagining.

All of these are important issues related to the illegal sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway. How these various issues will unfold is not only deeply related to our country, but also has a great impact on the safety of the entire East Asia. Therefore, we must not ignore it.

### Abyssinia Requests League of Nations Intervention; Negotiations with Italy Break Down 22

(Geneva) Negotiations between Italy and Abyssinia to resolve the dispute have now broken down, and the clouds of war are once again hanging over North Africa. The Secretariat of the League of Nations has received a telegram from the Abyssinian government, learning of the latest developments. People here are greatly disturbed by this. The Abyssinian government's telegram urges the League of Nations to deal with the Abyssinian request based on Article 11 of the League of Nations Covenant as soon as possible. After diplomatic negotiations stalled in mid-January, Abyssinia appealed to the League of Nations based on this article. In order to consider Abyssinia's application, the Council of the League of Nations, which was originally scheduled to meet in May, will probably be convened in advance. (Reuters, 18th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations today received another request from the King of Abyssinia to intervene in the dispute between his country and Italian Somaliland. At the same time, the situation on the border between the two countries is dangerous. It is said that Italy continues to send troops and equipment to Somaliland. Currently, there are more than 10,000 well-trained motorized elite soldiers bordering Abyssinia. The League of Nations recently sent a committee to the capital of Abyssinia to investigate the current situation in order to suggest a peaceful solution. However, today's request from Abyssinia is for the Council of the League of Nations to intervene immediately. According to reports, the King of Abyssinia has also repeatedly written to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, stating that Abyssinia has nothing to do with the Wal Wal incident. However, Italy continues to send troops to East Africa without stopping. Currently, more than tens of thousands of Italian troops are stationed on the border of Abyssinia, and there are 25,000 indigenous troops. Although Abyssinia also has 100,000 troops, their military equipment is poor and they are not the enemy of the Italian army. (National Telegram, 18th)

### Simon Announces in the House of Commons That a Note Has Been Presented to Germany; Consultations Were Held with France and Italy in Advance; Germany Expresses Its Willingness to Cooperate in the Future; Obstacles to Returning to the League of Nations Have Been Removed 23

(London) Foreign Secretary Simon participated in a cabinet meeting this morning to discuss the issue of German rearmament. Afterwards, he went to the House of Commons and announced that the government had instructed the British ambassador in Berlin to deliver a note to the German government this afternoon. The contents of the note cannot be disclosed before the German Foreign Minister receives it, but it will be announced as soon as he receives it. The government has consulted with the French and Italian governments on the issue of German rearmament, Simon said. After Simon finished speaking, opposition leader Lansbury asked whether the government would discuss this matter with the United States and other signatory countries of the treaty, or request a meeting of the League of Nations. Simon replied that these matters are currently under consideration by the government. Although the contents of the British government's note to Germany have not been disclosed by the authorities, everyone believes that it must contain some inquiries, with the aim of understanding the future attitude of Germany's foreign policy, especially whether Germany is still prepared to participate in collective security methods. This morning's cabinet meeting lasted for one hour and fifteen minutes. The cabinet met at 10:30 in the morning, half an hour earlier than usual. The crowd gathered on Downing Street retreated after being driven back by the police when cabinet members arrived. The cabinet members all looked happy. Foreign Secretary Simon stayed at the Foreign Office for a long time before going out to meet at the Prime Minister's residence across the street. He had a smile on his face when he left the Foreign Office. (Reuters, 18th)

(London) It is generally believed that the British cabinet meeting this morning decided to submit two questions to the German government and ask it to answer: (1) Is Germany prepared to return to the League of Nations? (2) Is Germany determined to participate in the security and consultation system under the leadership of the League of Nations? According to reports, at yesterday's meeting of the cabinet disarmament problem committee, two observations were made on Germany's decision to implement conscription and increase military spending. On the one hand, the restoration of conscription in Germany was regarded as a clear violation of the Treaty of Versailles. On the other hand, the establishment of 36 divisions in the German army was considered to exceed the limit of equality required by Germany, and the number of troops was more than that of Germany's neighboring countries. The cabinet meeting today reaffirmed these observations. The British note to Germany will specifically raise the above two points. Regarding this note, the government will issue a statement in the House of Commons this afternoon. (Havas, 18th)

(Paris) According to recent news from Rome, it has been confirmed that the Italian government has agreed to the French proposal regarding the situation caused by Germany's decision to restore military freedom and establish a compulsory conscription system. Italy supports the joint protest of the British, French and Italian ambassadors in Germany, and Italy also advocates that the three countries consult with each other. As for submitting this matter to the League of Nations for handling, Italy does not express any objection, but believes that it should be submitted to the League of Nations after the results of consultations between the United Kingdom, France and Italy. In addition, the British government's views will be officially learned tonight. However, it is generally believed that the current situation is very serious, and there will be no more differences in the opinions of the United Kingdom, France and Italy. After the three governments exchange opinions, they will definitely produce a common program on how to deal with Germany's rash decision. (Havas, 18th)

(Berlin) The German side ignores the comments of foreign newspapers and the claim in French newspapers that France, Britain and Italy will issue a joint note protesting Germany's conscription system, because Germany's determination will never be shaken by external events and criticisms. On the contrary, Germany is now waiting quietly for the development of the situation and revealing its position, that is, Germany has already launched a campaign to sweep away the unequal treatment of the Treaty of Versailles. From now on, it will be happy to cooperate with all countries to create a new and peaceful Europe. Responsible parties here unanimously insist that the German army will be a defender of peace, and will never forget it. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Paris) According to news from Berlin, Germany has obtained equal status in the military, so it feels that there are no more obstacles to returning to the League of Nations. (Reuters, 18th)

### Hitler and Blomberg Explain the Purpose of Conscription 24

(Berlin) The whole world is feeling uneasy due to Germany's conscription system. Head of State Hitler issued a book to the world today, stating that Germany does not want war. What our people seek is only the opportunity to live and work in peace and contentment. However, there is really no way to continue to survive under the humiliation of the Treaty of Versailles. Believe me, the joy of our people today does not hide any malice or ambitions of aggression against any country. We do not believe that Germany's actions can increase the crisis of war, etc. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Berlin) Commander-in-Chief of the National Defense Forces Blomberg declared in Berlin today when commemorating the fallen soldiers of the European War that no civilized country in the world has sacrificed as much life or endured as much pain as Germany in the four years of the European War. Therefore, the responsibility of those who died later is also heavier than that of the Germans. If we do not know how to repay our gratitude, then all the souvenirs are the same as official documents. Blomberg then traced back the suffering Germany has experienced since the Great War, and the revival after Hitler came to power, and said that since the promulgation of the conscription system, the German government has created a new foundation for security. Germany's army and navy will be no different from those of that year. Internally, military education and the spirit of sacrificing for the country will be instilled in young people. Externally, it will be Germany's defender and strive for equal rights for Germany. Our ideal should be a strong armed and self-respecting Germany, which will never again sign treaties that humiliate the country. But we should also keep in mind the lessons that the Great War taught us and avoid a second world war, because we must save ourselves and the future of Germany. If a second world war breaks out, Europe will not be enough to be a battlefield, and culture cannot be destroyed by modern warfare. We Germans do not seek a war of revenge, because the good name we have earned in the four years of the Great War is enough to shine in history. If the natural law that dominates all nations is still worth considering, then we believe that Europe and the world have the possibility of peaceful transformation. (National Telegram, 17th)

### Germany Wants to Use Established Facts as the Basis for Future Negotiations 25

(Berlin) Today's diplomatic and political commentary newspaper of the government agency published an article detailing the meaning of Germany's implementation of conscription. The newspaper first stated, "After a country is completely disarmed, will it not be invaded by neighboring countries? This is something that is absolutely not guaranteed. Therefore, the German cabinet's decision to implement a national conscription system is actually due to the most basic survival of a strong country. In recent years, although Germany's rights, such as self-defense and security, have been repeatedly declared by various countries, and its equal status has been unanimously recognized by various countries, the distance between empty talk and reality has increased day by day, and the environment has become increasingly evil. Therefore, to this day, the German government's actions should not be regarded as sudden by fair and impartial observers in the world. Even in terms of time, the current environment is also appropriate, because in the past few months, Germany has quietly watched the rapid expansion of their military equipment by the major powers in Europe. Among these powers, some are bound by treaties and clearly promised to reduce military preparations, or at least not to increase the total number of troops, and these countries are all participants in the disarmament conference. In terms of moral concepts, there is no reason to increase military equipment, but their actions to increase military equipment are clearly visible to everyone. Today's Germany, in order to stare at the facts, has to place the defense of the country in a natural, broader and more basic last country. What is even more important is that Germany's military reorganization, to its extreme, is only reaching a low level of military equipment, and it is only the beginning of the recent arms race among the powers. Therefore, Germany's actions, although not to be taken as isolated actions, are not to attack everyone, but to advance. On the contrary, this is the beginning of healthy development. The appropriate balance that Europe has lacked in the past fifteen years, and the unease and crisis caused by this defect, can now be eliminated in one fell swoop. Therefore, the establishment of equality in national defense will be a clear basis for future negotiations. All relevant countries should rely on existing realities. Germany has been and is willing to accept any restrictions, but it depends on whether other powers are willing to receive the same treatment. In a word, what Germany requires is nothing more than equal status among equal countries." (National Telegram, 17th)

(Berlin) Regarding the issue of German rearmament, according to those familiar with the political situation here, Article 5 of the Treaty of Versailles stipulates that Germany must disarm, and Article 8 stipulates that other countries must also reduce their military equipment. Sixteen years have passed since the conclusion of the treaty. The German side has long complied with the treaty and reduced its military equipment to the scope allowed by the treaty. However, other countries have made a lot of noise about the danger to security and have tried their best to reorganize their military affairs. According to the facts, such as the recent publication of the British White Paper, the extension of the French military service years, and even the expansion of the Soviet Union's army to 960,000 people, Germany is located in the center of Europe and is surrounded by enemies on all sides. Since others do not comply with the treaty, Germany is not willing to lag behind in order to defend the security of its territory. In particular, after the head of state Hitler returned to the country in Saar, he solemnly stated that there would be no territorial dispute with France in the future. At this point, those who feared Germany could be relieved. However, others do not understand, and they all take military competition as a matter of course. In fact, the facts are as described above. The reason for Germany's rearmament is partly due to the fact that others do not comply with the treaty, and the important thing is that it is purely for self-defense in order to maintain world peace. (National Telegram, 18th)

### German Conscription System Announced 26

(Berlin) According to an announcement by the authorities today, the new compulsory military service will officially conscript the first batch of new recruits on April 1. Men born in 1914 are also included. The term of military service will not exceed 12 months. All men from 21 to 25 years old must be conscripted. Men from 25 to 30 years old will be reserve soldiers and will receive six weeks of military training every two years. (Reuters, 18th)

### German Memorial for Fallen Soldiers; Berlin Resembles a Large Military Camp 27

(Berlin) This morning, the grandest military ceremony since the European War was held at the National Theater. At an early hour, the whole city heard the sound of marching troops and the sound of cavalry hooves. Hitler's personal black guard was lined up on both sides of the road leading to the hospital. Those who attended the ceremony included former Crown Prince Wilhelm, Head of State Hitler, General Mackensen, General Goering, and other government officials. Defense Minister Blomberg gave a speech to the audience to commemorate the German soldiers who died in the European War. The British, French, and Italian ambassadors did not attend, but the US ambassador and the aviation and military members of the British ambassador's office were present. Blomberg said that if there is a world war today, it would be equivalent to self-destruction. What Germans want is peace and to enjoy the equal rights and equal security of all nations. After the meeting, the crowd went to the square in front of the old Berlin residence. Military bands were gathered in the field to play music. Seventy flag bearers of the National Defense Forces marched in goose steps to the front of the viewing platform, where Head of State Hitler, General Goering, and other high-ranking military officers saluted the National Socialist Party. At that time, a field artillery team fired 24 salutes. Then the crowd went to the tomb of the Unknown Soldier to lay wreaths in tribute. After the ceremony, Hitler took a plane to Munich and drove through the streets where thousands of people gathered on both sides to review the entire army of Bavaria. Before the review ceremony was held, a car drove into the square at the intersection. The driver accidentally turned to the side of the road. At that time, Hitler was standing there, planning to step onto the viewing platform opposite. Everyone was worried when they saw this, but no one dared to make a sound. It took 30 seconds before it stopped. Then two black guards came and stood on the footboard of the car, waving for the driver to drive away. Who was in the car was not announced. (Reuters, 17th)

### British Newspapers Criticize but Remain Calm 30

(London) None of the British morning newspapers failed to criticize Germany's decision to expand its military equipment, but few made alarmist remarks. Some newspapers debated whether Foreign Secretary Simon should postpone his trip to Germany. Several other newspapers attached great importance to the words of German Defense Minister Blomberg that Europe is too small and cannot be a second battlefield, that war is a way of self-destruction, and that Germany wants to establish a new order in Europe and the world by peaceful means. The Morning Post stated that this week's incidents showed the futility of relying on written guarantees. Hitler's brown shirts are no different from Caesar's military uniforms, both discarding the principle of Germanic power. Disarmament is now hopeless, but the pursuit of peaceful cooperation should not be abandoned because of this. The Daily Express stated that Germany's declaration should not be regarded as a challenge to further expand military equipment, but should be regarded as a renewed and serious effort to seek universal disarmament, because the way to obtain peace lies in collective guarantees, not in collective military equipment. The Daily Mail stated that there is no reason to panic now. Hitler's actions are just changing the brand. The Exchange News stated that the German government's announcement of the new compulsory military investment law today is extremely untimely, because what is urgently needed now is a meeting of responsible leaders of the countries concerned. The Daily Telegraph stated that the German government has deliberately destroyed the old basis for negotiations. If it does not suggest a new basis for negotiations, then Britain will not send Simon to visit Berlin. If Germany demands an absolute minimum of 36 divisions, then there will be no hope for a military agreement between France and Germany, and the so-called security will become a bubble again. The Times stated that if Hitler's actions are only a way to seek equality, then the harm is not irreparable, and Foreign Secretary Simon should visit Berlin according to the original plan. British policy does not fluctuate constantly. Its purpose is to form a collective system to protect Europe's security. If this hope still exists, then it will not abandon its work. However, what Hitler himself must hear urgently is whether Germany sincerely wants to participate in this system and carry out an equal plan to limit military equipment. The Financial Times stated that as far as the London market is concerned, only a calm attitude should be maintained. The Daily Express stated that the National Socialist Party government is now using this move to express its desire to restore the lost legal benefits and land by force. When Britain encounters this crisis, it should no longer be involved in the broken treaties, but place its sea, land and air forces to become the strongest country in the world other than the United States. A Reuters diplomatic reporter stated that the entire foundation of the international military system that everyone hopes can replace the Treaty of Versailles now seems to be destroyed by Germany's actions. The issue of Simon and Eden's visits should be reconsidered due to the changing situation. However, in any case, Eden will eventually visit Russia and Poland. According to qualified observers in London, Germany can still participate in a collective security plan, but what its Minister of Propaganda Goebbels said that Germany's national defense must be handled by Germany's own power in the future can be considered an ominous sign. It is heard that the French government has sent a note to the British government through its ambassador in the United Kingdom, explaining France's views on Germany's actions and suggesting that discussions should be started immediately to deal with the new situation. A Reuters report from Paris stated that French officials seemed to advocate submitting the German matter to the League of Nations, but this proposal has not yet been decided. People in Paris believe that Germany's recent actions to violate the treaty cannot be ignored without protest. As for what kind of protest, it depends on the consultation between the United Kingdom, France, and Italy. However, since Germany's actions are related to other countries that signed the Treaty of Versailles, the most appropriate way to handle this matter is to do it in Geneva. French Prime Minister Flandin will make a statement on Germany's restoration of military equipment in the House of Commons on Tuesday. (Reuters, 18th)

Foreign Press Advocates for International Cooperation 32

(Paris) Following Germany's violation of the Treaty of Versailles military clauses and its unauthorized reinstatement of compulsory military service, the newspapers here are generally advocating that the great powers should urgently form a coalition to safeguard peace, to prevent solemn treaties from being openly violated without penalty, and to ensure European order. In particular, they are calling for close cooperation between Britain, France, and Italy. *Le Petit Parisien* stated, "The great powers' initial reaction to Germany's move is almost certain to be a strong protest to Germany by their ambassadors stationed there. However, the governments of the other nations may also issue solemn declarations stating the seriousness of Germany's actions. As for British Foreign Secretary Simon's visit to Germany, if it proceeds as originally planned, it is feared that it will not yield any results, as Germany has clearly opposed the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact. Conversely, French Foreign Minister Laval's proposed visit to Moscow is widely anticipated." *Le Journal* stated, "In 1914, before the start of the Great War, Germany predicted that Britain would not interfere in continental European affairs and thus dared to initiate hostilities. If Germany is to be prevented from repeating its old tricks, the only effective method is for the great powers to form a sober and resolute coalition, which may perhaps succeed." *L'Echo de Paris* regretted Britain's hesitancy and indecision, stating, "Germany always benefits from the hesitation and indecision of the great powers, and this case is no different." (Havas dispatch, 18th)

Russian Newspaper Discusses Germany's Accelerated War Preparations 33

(Moscow) *Izvestia's* lead article discusses Germany's implementation of universal conscription, stating, "The Soviet Union is not a signatory to the Treaty of Versailles, so it need not analyze this major event from a diplomatic or legal perspective. Our concern is limited solely to its political significance. It is a great mistake to say that since German armaments already exist, the cancellation of the Treaty of Versailles is merely a formality and a gesture. Germany's implementation of universal conscription today and its declaration of rearmament are precisely intended to achieve its profound practical goals. Therefore, what was said above is not correct. Germany today is rejecting all conventions, declaring its freedom to reorganize its armaments, with the aim of acquiring the military technology it has created in the last two years in the shortest possible time. Therefore, what we see is Germany's accelerated war preparations.

"Negotiations between Germany and the British Foreign Secretary are imminent, and negotiations with France will follow. Germany's unilateral departure from the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles comes exactly one week before the start of Anglo-German negotiations. This move is a provocation to those powers willing to recognize Germany's equal rights in a general security organization. This step has a great political purpose. Britain, France, and Italy are willing to lift restrictions on German armaments in exchange for political constraints that would limit Germany's aggressive policies. At the same time, they plan to compromise with Germany on the amount of armaments. However, Germany responded with a declaration of universal conscription, implying that the amount of German armaments has been determined by Germany itself. Therefore, it need not assume any obligations in the security realm in exchange for concessions made to it on the armaments issue. Therefore, the purpose of Germany's move is to ensure that Germany bears no obligations in the security realm. German imperialism will select a sacrificial victim to test its iron fist. Therefore, this move is a preparation for war in the political sense. "Germany's policy is entirely created by the policies of the great powers themselves (first and foremost, Britain). They endorse Germany and encourage the leaders of German policy, saying, 'Now is the time to take risks,' and indicating to them that any action is permissible. For example, Germany's proposal to negotiate separately with Britain, to strike at the Anglo-French front, as a response to the Anglo-French proposal of February 3, was actually accepted. Again, when all parties asked Germany to participate in an organization to safeguard peace in Europe, Germany responded by refusing to promote peace, but the response Germany received was a palliative, implying that they could certainly reach some compromise, as if war and peace could truly be compromised. Thus, German diplomacy has a belief that they can exchange promises. To confirm this belief, Germany initially asked Foreign Secretary Simon to postpone his visit to Germany, a move that had never been seen in diplomatic history. However, the response was a gentle and agreeable tone. Then Germany made its penultimate move: regardless of the prohibitions of the Treaty of Versailles, it declared that it would set up an air force from April 1, and this move was also accepted. So what shame will Germany have in its policies? It not only thwarts its enemies, but it also has a greater victory at home, namely, raising the tide of German nationalism and consolidating the position of the fascist government in war preparations. We certainly know that the speed of Germany's rearmament and its firm rejection of various diplomatic conventions are all symbols of Germany's preparations for actual action. Will its goal be Austria? (Hitler recently said that the German question must be resolved in the same way as the Saar question.) Danzig? (Although Danzig is not German territory, its President of the Senate attached the words "Hail Hitler" to the end of his government documents.) Or Memel? No one can say. However, one thing is absolutely certain: Germany's recent actions have predetermined its political aggression.

"In this situation, everything depends on the attitude of the powers against whom Germany's policies are directed. If they can quickly form an organization for mutual assistance once Germany initiates aggression, and if Berlin can understand that this organization will materialize whether Germany wishes to join it or not, then it will realize that Germany alone cannot stand against a coalition of powers willing to maintain peace. "Time waits for no one; there must be no hesitation or indecision. The question today is that Germany has already stated its goals, so the other nations should immediately state their means of defense and their ability to defend the peace of Europe and all mankind." (TASS dispatch, 18th)

Japanese Newspaper Believes Europe is in a State of Unease 34

(Tokyo) Japanese authorities have not yet received official information from Berlin regarding the matter of Germany's military rearmament, and therefore have not issued any comments. However, the general public believes that this is entirely a European issue, so the Japanese government will adopt a policy of quiet observation. As for what repercussions this matter will have in the Far East, that will depend on its development. Japanese newspapers have published lengthy commentaries on Hitler's declaration. *Asahi Shimbun* expressed regret over the attitude Germany is now taking, fearing that it will provoke international sentiment. However, the newspaper does not believe that Hitler's actions will lead to a new crisis in Europe. It continued that French policy is fickle and inconsistent, on the one hand expressing trust in the League of Nations, on the other hand calling on European nations to resist Germany. The nations involved, such as France and Britain, should now use their political talents to find ways to overcome difficulties and improve international relations, and should not merely interpret treaties rigidly. *Hochi Shimbun* advised Germany to achieve its national aspirations through moderate methods, and advised the nations involved to treat Germany more generously. However, *Nichinichi Shimbun* held a fearful view, stating that Germany's rearmament, even if it does not lead to war, will put Europe in a state of great unease. (Reuters dispatch, 18th)

Australia to Strengthen Armaments, Emphasizing Air Force 35

(London) The Associated Press learned today that increasing Australia's armaments will be the second step in the British Empire's long-term defense plan. May 6, the 50th anniversary of the British monarch's accession to the throne, will be an appropriate opportunity for officials from the self-governing dominions to gather in London to discuss and promote security plans. Since Japan announced the abrogation of the Washington Naval Treaty, which will expire on December 31, 1936, Britain is actively planning the Empire's security, with a particular focus on the Pacific region. The initial concrete plan for this matter is Australia's ten-year military reform plan. Sir Tingey, Secretary of the Defence Committee, inspected South Africa, Australia, New Zealand, and Canada for a long time and held meetings with the authorities and military commanders. He returned to London on January 6. Over the past few weeks, he has discussed the results of his trip with cabinet members. According to expert observations, particular attention will be paid to strengthening the Australian Air Force and using it to resist attacks from the sea. As for restoring conscription, it will provoke opposition. Infantry is also not suitable for Australia. Both are reasons for promoting increased air defense capabilities. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Greece Clarifies Internal Affairs 37

Athens: Prime Minister Tsaldaris and Metaxas, the minister without portfolio representing right-wing forces, have reached an agreement on the government's program of action for internal affairs. Prime Minister Tsaldaris believes that although the government must take active measures to clarify internal affairs, the government's actions should be within the legal scope. Land Minister Kondylis also holds the same view. The only things that the government has firmly decided on now are the abolition of the Senate, the increase of executive power, and the purge of party elements from the army and administrative organs. However, the method of implementing these reforms has not yet been decided. Some people advocate holding a popular referendum to avoid the convening of a national assembly to amend the constitution, as demanded by some political parties. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

Franco-Belgian Paris Conference Decides to Jointly Defend the Gold Standard; Belgian Government Announces Nationalization of Cash; Establishes Exchange Office to Manage Exchange Rates 38

(Paris) Franco-Belgian talks began this morning and ended at night. Minutes after the talks ended, the Belgian cabinet members set off on their return to Brussels. According to an official statement, Belgian Prime Minister Theunis stated the reforms in the economic and monetary situation. The French and Belgian governments unanimously advocate taking appropriate steps to protect the currencies of the gold bloc countries from speculative attacks, while also seeking to develop mutual trade relations between the gold bloc countries. In addition to the financial negotiations, French Foreign Minister Laval and Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans also discussed various diplomatic issues. Furthermore, Belgian cabinet members indicated that the interdependence of the gold standard countries has always been Belgium's main perspective. Therefore, the main purpose of this Franco-Belgian talk is to obtain some trade benefits from France, especially such as the most-favored-nation clauses. It is hoped that changes will be made to those that harm Franco-Belgian trade, and the French side is also suffering from the increase in import surpluses. Therefore, they are quite considering further cooperation in trade with the gold standard countries. (Havas dispatch, 17th)

Brussels: The Belgian government announced this morning the establishment of a central exchange office to maintain the Belgian currency. In the future, all foreign exchange transactions will be managed by this office. Except for remittances for the price of imported goods, all other remittances are prohibited. Ordinary commercial drafts must be paid by this office or the National Bank. Only this office and the National Bank have the right to transport gold and silver bullion into and out of Belgium. This regulation takes effect immediately. According to this order, the Belgian Prime Minister Theunis, French Prime Minister Flandin, and other financial experts met last night. In the past week, the Belgian currency has fallen sharply in the world's financial markets, threatening the situation of the gold bloc countries. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Brussels: Today's semi-official announcement states that all gold transactions, whether in bars or coins, must be managed to prevent hoarding of gold coins. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

(Paris) According to backstage news, a Belgian railway loan of 24 million pounds will be raised next week in order to maintain the Belgian franc. (Reuters dispatch, 17th)

(Paris) The Associated Press learned today from Brussels that the National Bank of France will lend money to the National Bank of Belgium, so that the Belgian bank can cope with the attacks of speculators around the world on the Belgian currency. It is said that this loan is not cash, but a credit method, freely controlled by the Belgian bank. As the National Bank of Belgium's foreign currency reserves have long been exhausted, the Belgian Prime Minister Theunis, Foreign Minister Hymans, and National Bank President Franqui met last night with French Prime Minister Flandin and Finance Minister Lamoureux, and agreed that France would provide a loan. The representatives of the two countries have resolved that the gold bloc countries must do their best to maintain the status quo when the British pound falls. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

(Paris) International observers predict that after the release of this statement, there will be a reaction in the world financial market, because the leaders of Wall Street in New York are showing great concern about the Belgian currency crisis. (National News Agency dispatch, 18th)

Japan Establishes Cabinet Deliberation Council; Establishes Emergency Policy; House of Representatives Discussed Yesterday 42

(Tokyo) The House of Representatives Budget Committee began discussing the Cabinet Deliberation Council issue at around 11:00 AM today. The exchange between Kiyose Kiyoo and Prime Minister Okada was as follows: Kiyose asked, what is the reason for establishing the Cabinet Deliberation Council? Prime Minister Okada replied, to establish national policies for the current emergency. Kiyose asked, have you considered the issue of the return of party politics? The Prime Minister replied, the Cabinet Deliberation Council has nothing to do with party politics. Kiyose asked, then is the establishment of the Cabinet Deliberation Council a strengthening of the non-partisan cabinet?

The Prime Minister replied, no, it is an organ for establishing national plans for the next century. Kiyose asked, what are the so-called important national policies deliberated by the Council? The Prime Minister replied, issues of local autonomy, central and local finances, and the reorganization of tax revenues. Kiyose asked, can't these issues be agreed upon in the cabinet? The Prime Minister replied, the cabinet cannot decide on important national policies, so this Cabinet Deliberation Council is specifically used as a advisory body. Kiyose asked, the opinions within the cabinet should be controlled by the Prime Minister, so is the establishment of the Cabinet Deliberation Council forgetting the Prime Minister's responsibility? The Prime Minister replied, the cabinet is not unable to establish important national policies. The establishment of the Deliberation Council can make the relationships between various ministries smoother. Kiyose asked, isn't the Deliberation Council making the relationships between the various ministries smoother an act of overreach? Is the Prime Minister trying to avoid taking responsibility? The Prime Minister replied, all responsibility should be borne by the Prime Minister. Kiyose asked, establishing such an organ after the Okada Cabinet was formed can be said to expose the cabinet's lack of management and lack of confidence. Isn't the establishment of national policy deliberation like building a house on top of a house? The Prime Minister replied, it cannot be said to be building a house on top of a house because it is established under the cabinet (the entire room laughed).

Kiyose also asked about military and diplomatic issues. A recess was taken at 1:18 PM. The meeting continued at 1:00 PM in the afternoon, with Nakatani Sadayori raising questions about the Cabinet Deliberation Council issue. The questions and answers are recorded below:

Q: How should the cases decided by the Deliberation Council be handled? Judging from this situation, isn't the cabinet losing its unity? Why was the budget, which is so important and includes such significant policies, delayed until today?

Prime Minister: Due to various circumstances, it has been delayed until now. I should certainly apologize.

Q: In any case, the second reserve fund, which cannot be avoided, and the budget of the Cabinet Deliberation Council are combined into one, and you also want to pass it. Is this delay due to this impure thinking?

Prime Minister: There is absolutely no impure thinking.

Q: Is the Cabinet Deliberation Council permanent?

Prime Minister: Because it is for establishing national plans, a permanent nature is preferable. If the cabinet changes and the council also changes with it, it would be meaningless.

Q: Why not adopt a system without any grand strategies? Finance Minister Takahashi is said to have also held this view. Is this true? What is his opinion?

Finance Minister: I also held this view, but now it has been decided that the Deliberation Council is the most suitable. Hoshijima Nijiro (Seiyu) asked the following question: The composition of the Cabinet Deliberation Council is neither like the Brain Trust in the United States nor like the Economic General Staff in Germany, but most similar to the State Planning Committee in the Soviet Union. At a time when parliamentary politics are reviving, there is such an uninteresting situation. I wonder what your thoughts are? The Prime Minister replied, the Cabinet Deliberation Council is definitely not like the above, and it does not hinder the powers of the parliament, etc. (United Press dispatch, 18th)

--March 18th, Reuters Exclusive Business Report-- 88

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price: Today, due to the instability of the exchange market, it rose one shilling and six pence to one hundred and forty-six shillings and eleven pence.

London Silver Market: Today, the silver price rose due to the weakness of the pound sterling. Spot is twenty-seven pence three-seven-five, which is higher than Saturday by two-five. Futures are twenty-seven pence four-three-seven-five, higher by one-eight-seven-five. The United States bought in the morning, India sold, and China bought and sold. The closing market was stable.

Mumbai Silver Market: The market was weak and stable this afternoon. The opening price of spot was 65 rupees, which was three annas higher than the previous opening. The closing continued to rise two and one anna, reaching 65 rupees two annas.

Mountley Silver: The opening price of futures rose by about twenty-five pounds.

Exchange Rates

British and American: In the London foreign exchange market, European countries competed to purchase US dollars to offset the recent sales of francs and Belgian francs. The exchange market was quite turbulent. As a result, the pound sterling fell sharply, with the US dollar being more affected than the French franc. The opening price of the British-American exchange rate was four dollars seven corners eight and two-five cents, which was two and three-seven-five cents lower than the closing price on Saturday. Within half an hour of the opening, the price fell sharply, reaching four dollars seven corners five and two-five cents at half past ten, three cents lower than the opening. Thereafter, the market situation stabilized slightly due to the authorities' use of the equalization fund. At eleven o'clock, it returned to four dollars seven corners five and a half cents. Subsequently, there was a rebound. At two o'clock in the afternoon, the price was four dollars seven corners seven and seven-five cents, half a cent lower than the opening.

British and French: The opening price was 72 francs 59, down thirty-one pounds. At half past ten, it shrank another fifty-three pounds to 72 francs 06. The market situation improved later, rising nine pounds at noon and another nineteen pounds at one o'clock in the afternoon, reaching 72 francs 34. It did not move at two o'clock.

American and British: The New York foreign exchange market was chaotic this morning. The opening price of the British exchange rate was four dollars seven corners seven and three-seven-five cents, down three and two-five cents, and then fell to four dollars seven corners six and six-two-five cents. The opening price of the French exchange rate was six dollars five corners nine and six-two-five cents, up three-seven-five cents.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton Market: It was expected that the price would not change much today. However, after the opening, European countries and Liverpool sold one after another, causing the price to fall by more than thirty pounds. This kind of fall came suddenly and completely unexpectedly. Within half an hour of the opening, the price continued to fall by sixteen pounds in one block, a net drop of fifty pounds compared to the closing price on Saturday.

Chicago Wheat: The opening price fell. There was news of a sandstorm in the southwest, so the market price rose slightly. However, the stock market was weak, and the wheat market still had a falling trend within the first half hour, but the fall was limited to zero.

Mumbai Cotton Market: Speculators bought in, but European exporters sold. The closing price of white Lorch cotton for April and May was 222 rupees, one and a half rupees lower than the closing price on Saturday.

Liverpool Wheat: At one o'clock this afternoon, the price for May was five shillings and one-eight-seven-five, which was two and five higher than the closing price on Saturday.

Liverpool Cotton: At one o'clock in the afternoon, the price for May was six pence one-three, down fourteen pounds.

Rubber

London: Today, the market price fell one-eight-seven-five. This is also because the exchange rate is falling and chaotic three-seven-five, which is one-eight-seven-five lower than the closing price on Saturday. The popularity is relatively loose.

New York: Today, the market price was affected by poor communications from London. The opening price fell by about seventy pounds. Although some people bought in when the price fell within half an hour, the falling trend has not stopped.

Securities

New York: After the opening of the market today, sales entrustment orders came one after another, and there was no time to deal with them, resulting in a general decline. Troop Transfers in Chaozhou Lead to Increased Bandit Activity 106

Shantou Correspondence: Recently, taking advantage of troop transfers in the Chaozhou region, bandits have been increasingly active. Local guard units are understaffed and struggling to cope. On the 11th evening, the village of Xinbei, near Chiliao in the Guiyu district of Chaoyang County, was suddenly attacked by 160 Communist bandits, including more than 30 female Communists, all with short hair, dressed in military uniforms, and armed with machine guns and Mauser pistols. They stormed the village watchtower, disarming the guards and seizing 14 rifles. The police force hastily engaged in battle, sounding gongs to alert neighboring villages for assistance. However, due to the late hour and strong winds, nearby villages did not hear the alarm. The bandits fired on the watchtower and then broke into the home of villager Liu Hudi, looting everything and kidnapping Liu to Beishan. Furthermore, Huang Huishen, a resident of Shifo Village, who ran a Western medicine shop in Chijiao, was kidnapped by two female Communists while passing through the Nanshanke area of Shibi. Huang managed to escape halfway and reported that there were many bandits in Beishan. After the departure of Zhong’s regiment from Raoping County, on the evening of the 7th, bandits armed with Mauser pistols gathered five miles southwest of the city, plotting to attack. They posted reactionary slogans overnight. At that time, a unit of Ye's regiment arrived from Shangrao and immediately sounded bugles, mobilizing the police force to be on high alert. Seeing that the relief troops had arrived, the bandits dared not attack the city. The city is rife with prostitutes, making it easy to harbor criminals. The council has resolved to expel itinerant prostitutes from the territory. Moreover, Rong Village, at the border of Chao’an and Shaoping, was stormed by dozens of bandits on the evening of the 10th, attempting to loot. The deputy village chief led a team to engage the bandits, who also opened fire, resulting in a fierce battle lasting an hour. The bandits were overwhelmed and fled into the nearby forest. During the attack, two villagers were kidnapped, but the village chief led a team in pursuit, and the bandits released them. The following night, Shiken Village was also looted by bandits, with a large number of people kidnapped. According to visitors from Raoping, recently many bandits from the Fujian border have infiltrated the Purao area. On the morning of the 7th, 67 laborers transporting goods in the Fenghuang district went to Chao’an city to buy groceries. While passing through Dashui Creek in the Shangrong district, at the border of Chaozhou and Raoping, a known haunt of Communist bandits, all the goods being transported were robbed by the bandits, who fled into the mountains. The porters and vendors cried out in misery along the way. This is the latest situation. Furthermore, a group of Communist bandits, numbering over 300, infiltrated the Fengshun area of the Tiandong district via Chao’an, heavily armed with guns and cannons. They have yet to be suppressed. These individuals claim to be an anti-Japanese army, with strong political overtones. They attempted to borrow over 10,000 yuan from the Chenghuang business association for military expenses, but the association refused. People in the surrounding area are quite fearful. After Chen Shuyiao's regiment took over defense of Fengshun, the defenses have been greatly strengthened. Regiment Commander Chen considers Fengshun to be the central hub of the Chaozhou and Meizhou counties and a historically vital military location, and has sent troops to build a ring road around the city, with a half-month deadline for completion, to aid in defense against bandits. In addition to building the road, the regiment has also banned people from bathing naked in the Tanghu hot springs during the day, expelled southern opera actresses, and designated locations outside the city for opium dens and gambling houses to maintain order. It is reported that the Fujian border is very unstable recently. Bandit leaders Zhang Dingcheng and female bandit Fan Lechun have returned to Changting from Ruichang, Jiangxi, commanding the Red bandits Deng Zhiwen, Qiu Jinsheng, and others, occupying Yongding, Shanghang, Qiling, Jinsha, and Lilongkeng. Ships on the Ting River to Fengshi and Hushi have been repeatedly intercepted and robbed, disrupting cargo transport between Fujian and Guangdong. This is a matter of great concern. An investigation reveals that most of the local Communist bandits in Chaozhou and Meizhou today infiltrated from the Fujian border and are taking advantage of troop transfers to increase their activity.

Bandit Suppression Completed in Central Anhui 107

Wuhu Correspondence: Since the elimination of the large-scale bandits in southern Anhui's Huizhou region, there has been another surge of banditry in central Anhui, including Hefei and Chaoxian. Governor Liu Zhenhuan has dispatched troops to suppress them. He also transferred Hu Peigeng, the security commander of the Yanhua Second District, from Wuhu to assist with the attack, and appointed Ge Yunlong as the commander for the suppression efforts in central Anhui, under unified command. Recently, the main force of the bandits has been defeated, with only a small number of bandits fleeing to remote areas near Hefei. The security forces under Commander Wang in Bengbu and the counties of Dingyuan and Quanjiao, as well as Zhao's troops under Ge, have made contact and plan to encircle and annihilate the remaining bandits. Those who were coerced into joining the bandits have been released and returned to their farms. It has come to light that the recent outbreak of banditry was largely due to famine and the manipulation of those affected. Military force can only address the symptoms; political solutions are needed to address the root cause. Some corrupt village leaders and local bullies were also found to be aiding the bandits. The provincial government has formulated measures to appease and resettle the displaced, recruit and investigate stray bandits, expedite emergency relief through work programs, strengthen self-defense and reorganize the baojia system, and prevent revenge killings, in order to protect people's lives and property. These measures have been communicated to all counties for strict implementation. Recently, Xu Tingyao, the head of the military group of the military transportation inspection delegation, whose hometown is Wuwei County in Anhui Province, learned about the frequent banditry in Anhui Province, as well as a mutiny by the security forces in Wuwei County. After arriving in Wuhu from Nanjing, he received news that order in Wuwei had been restored. Today, he went directly to Anqing to discuss matters with Governor Liu, and will then proceed to Wuhan and Sichuan to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and report on the situation. Since implementing the abolition of excessive taxes and levies, the provincial government has actively reorganized legitimate tax revenue. It has established the Anhui Province Tax Supervision Committee to eliminate corruption and avoid harassment. Prominent figures from both inside and outside the province, as well as leaders from various county chambers of commerce, have been invited to serve on the committee, including Xu Shiying and Wu Xingzhou. The provincial government considers the committee's role in the province's finances to be crucial and plans to formally establish it in the province soon. It has recently telegraphed the committee members to urge them to attend the inaugural meeting in the province. Wu Xingzhou departed yesterday with Cui Lianggong, a standing member of the Wuhu Chamber of Commerce. It is said that after the committee is established, its office will be moved to Wuhu for convenience. Xu Shiying, considering Wuhu to be Anhui's leading commercial hub, has also expressed his strong support for this proposal in a letter from Shanghai to Wuhu. The committee has the authority to directly make representations and suggestions to the provincial government regarding the management of taxes in the province and can directly appeal to the central government regarding any illegal or excessive taxes, to ensure that tax revenue goes to public use and that merchants are not subjected to illegal harassment. (16th)

Plague Outbreak in Guangxi Province 108

Meningitis Spreads Through Yong, Liu, Gui, and Luo; Quarantine Stations Established to Prevent Further Spread

Guangzhou Correspondence: Recently, there has been an outbreak of meningitis in Guangxi Province, with widespread transmission. The symptoms initially include chills and vomiting, followed by stiffness of the neck and sensitivity to light, and then fever. If the fever does not subside within a few days, the patient will die. The disease first broke out in Liuzhou and then spread to Luorong, Guilin, and Nanning. The number of deaths caused by the disease is countless. In recent days, officials and civilians in Guangxi Province have been extremely busy with prevention and control efforts. The military and provincial government have purchased a large batch of prophylactic serum, which is being distributed to military personnel, civilians, and government agencies for injection. At the same time, quarantine stations have been established in various locations to strictly inspect travelers. Any patient found to have the disease is immediately sent to a nearby hospital for isolation and treatment to prevent further transmission. The locations of the established quarantine stations and the hospitals responsible for conducting the quarantine are as follows: Nanning Zhennanning Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by the affiliated hospital of the Provincial Medical College, with the Provincial Public Security Bureau assisting; Xincheng Datang Railway Station Quarantine Station, assisted by the Xincheng County Government; Nanning Xixiangtang Road Quarantine Station, inspected by Guangxi Military Hospital; Lijiang Quarantine Station, inspected by the General Headquarters Military Hospital; Liuzhou Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by Liuzhou Military Hospital; Beicheng Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by the 43rd Division Military Hospital, also assisted by the Liuzhou Municipal Government; Liujiang Waterway Quarantine Station, inspected by Liuzhou Public Hospital; Datang Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by Wuzhou Provincial Hospital; Luorong County Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by the medical station of the 127th Regiment stationed in Luorong; Lipu Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by Guilin Provincial Hospital, assisted by the Lipu County Government; Guilin Railway Station Quarantine Station, inspected by the 45th Division Military Hospital; Guijiang Waterway Quarantine Station, inspected by the temporary hospital of the 15th Army, assisted by the Guilin County Government. The weekly inspection reports from each station are submitted weekly for review. The expenses of each station are temporarily covered by the respective county governments or public security bureaus and will be reimbursed after being reported and approved. Each quarantine station has been allocated a daily food allowance of 40 cents per medical staff member and 25 cents per patient from the date of establishment. In addition, the hospitals have already received the prophylactic serum issued by the government and, starting from the 11th of this month, will hold free prophylactic injections every afternoon at 1 p.m. to ensure public safety and prevent the spread of the epidemic. (March 13)

Two Opium Traffickers Arrested in Songjiang 110

The local anti-smoking committee, acting on instructions from the provincial anti-smoking committee, noted a significant discrepancy between the amount of officially sold opium in the county and the amount reported by opium smokers, indicating that private opium was rampant and undermining official sales. The committee was ordered to strictly investigate and arrest offenders to maintain the anti-smoking policy. Investigators Sun Zongxiang and Hu Qihao conducted an investigation. Investigator Sun discovered that opium was being transported to Songjiang by train this morning (the 18th) and, together with Investigator Hu and police chief Dong Futang, waited to apprehend the suspects. They found a man named Xiao Yang from out of town in the bottom of Liren Lane, and found a large package of private opium in his rickshaw. The package contained opium from various regions of Yunnan and Sichuan, all labeled as products of Zheng Qiaji Xiangtai, weighing 66 taels and 7 mace. The suspect and the evidence were seized and handed over to the anti-smoking committee for legal action. On the 17th, police officers from the Huayang Public Security Station searched the Huayang station of a long-distance bus and apprehended an opium trafficker named Zhong Xiaoguan, seizing 15 taels of Zheng Qiaji Sichuan opium. An elderly woman who was with him escaped on the spot. It is reported that they had brought the opium from Shanghai to Songjiang. Zhong was handed over to the Public Security Bureau and then transferred to the committee for legal action.

Large-Scale Prison Break 111

At 5:00 PM on the 18th, while the prisoners in Songjiang County Prison were being served dinner, they took advantage of the opportunity to tie up and assault the prison guards, and then rushed out en masse. They cut the prison's telephone lines and burst out of the main gate, scattering in different directions. Law enforcement officers chased after the prisoners near the south side of the courthouse and recaptured two of them. The prison officials were out and had not returned. It is reported that thirteen prisoners escaped. Apart from the two who were recaptured, eleven are still at large. The arresting authorities have dispatched personnel to hunt them down. The county government and court officials have entered the prison to conduct a roll call. The situation in the city is extremely tense. Further details will be reported.

Suzhou Silk Weaving Industry Representatives Petition in Nanjing 112

Silk weaving factories using power looms in the Suzhou area previously found that the total electric meter of the power plant was inaccurate and the current was speeding up, causing the motors of each factory to use more electricity than normal, resulting in significant losses. They repeatedly negotiated with the power plant to request a reduction in charges, arguing that the price per degree for motor electricity set by the power plant was more than one cent higher than the price set by the Qishuyan power plant, and should also be reduced to ease the burden on businesses. After several months without a resolution, the factories appointed representatives Liu Fuqing, Lu Jigao, She Wenqing, and three others to travel to Nanjing yesterday (the 18th) with a petition to the Construction Committee, Ministry of Interior, and Executive Yuan, among other agencies. If they are unsuccessful, they will organize the Suzhou Electrical Users Union to fight for their cause, with a strong determination to achieve their goal.

Suzhou-Mudu Highway Expected to Open Soon 113

Construction of the Suzhou-Mudu Highway (Suzhou to Mudu), which began some time ago, is nearly complete. All bridge and road surface work is expected to be finished within half a month. The Suzhou-Mudu Long-Distance Bus Company has purchased seven long-distance buses from England, which have already arrived in Shanghai and will soon be transported to Suzhou. The opening is currently scheduled for June 1st. The company believes that rickshaws should still be allowed to operate on the Suzhou-Mudu road after it opens, but horse-drawn carriages damage the road surface and are unhygienic, and should absolutely not be allowed. They submitted a request to the Construction Department yesterday (the 18th) to permanently ban horse-drawn carriages from using the road.

Wuxi Bandits and Local Militia in Fierce Night Battle 114

Near the Third Bridge on the Xicheng Road, around 7:00 PM the night before last, five bandits armed with pistols suddenly blocked the road and robbed pedestrians and vehicles. Someone reported this to the watch post of the Fifth District local defense militia. Director Gu led over a dozen militiamen to pursue and apprehend the bandits. Unexpectedly, the bandits openly opened fire to resist. Both sides engaged in a fierce battle for a long time. The bandits were gradually overwhelmed and fled into the river. The militiamen also swam after them. As a result, one bandit was captured, while the rest escaped. When questioned, the captured bandit identified himself as Huang Fengqi, 20 years old, from Dongyang, Zhejiang. The local defense militia planned to hand over the captured bandit to the county for interrogation today.

Efforts to Advocate for the Domestic Sale of Refined Salt 115

Salt is one of the necessities of daily life for residents and is widely sold. Since the introduction of refined salt, there has been competition in the market between official salt and refined salt, with disputes arising over sales territories. Later, the Ministry of Finance established a system, designating areas within commercial ports where refined salt could be freely bought and sold. In Wuxi, this area was defined as north of the Gongyun Bridge to Zhoushanbang, approaching the Jingyun Market area, east to Xiaofen Bridge, and west to Yishan, within a surrounding area of thirty-six square li, as the commercial port area. Refined salt merchants, seeking greater convenience, repeatedly appealed for permission to freely circulate and sell refined salt within the five counties of Suzhou, Songjiang, Changzhou, Zhenjiang, and Wuxi in the former Suzhou region. This was approved by the Fifth Plenary Session two years ago, with eight provisional measures being published and implemented. Now it is learned that over twenty groups in the city, including the wine and soy sauce, winemaking, restaurant, meat, bamboo, hat, and Jiande Association, are concerned that the sale of refined salt is being obstructed. The Salt Administration of the Ministry of Finance will soon send personnel to Wuxi to investigate salt affairs. Therefore, a meeting was held to decide to appoint representatives to jointly petition after the official arrives in Wuxi, requesting that the area for the sale of refined salt be maintained and that no obstacles be placed in the way.

Nanjing Lun Lingfei's Anatomical Charts on Display in Nanjing 120

The exhibition of anatomical charts by Lun Lingfei, secretary to Zhang Yunzhong of the Central Guoyi Museum, opened yesterday at the Overseas Chinese Reception Center in Gulou, Nanjing. Over a hundred charts are on display, arranged in ten groups according to physiological order, such as the Physiological System Analysis Chart, Meridian System Anatomical Chart, Zangfu Meridian System Anatomical Chart, and Bieluo and Qiaosi Anatomical Chart. The remaining six groups are divided into meridian transport, Mu Yuan, Sanjiao system, diagnosis of the cun, guan, and chi, meridian affiliation of muscles and bones, and affiliation of meridian tendons. All anatomical and physiological aspects are covered, based on the principles of the Inner Canon and supplemented by Western anatomy, providing a new comprehensive system. In the future, traditional Chinese medicine will have the benefit of anatomical clarity, a significant achievement. It is reported that the anatomical charts were all drawn by Ms. Lun Lingfei, secretary of the National Medical Secret Museum.

Real Estate Developers Discuss Issuing Currency Notes with a Total Value of 50 Million Yuan, Banking Sector Expresses Concerns About Feasibility 126

According to the Shen Times News Agency, several leading real estate developers in Shanghai, recognizing the current economic downturn and stagnant business, plan to revitalize the market through real estate ventures as a means of providing relief. A meeting was convened at 2:00 PM on the 17th at the residence of Cheng Linsheng, located at 1550 Jing'an Temple Road. Attendees included over eighty prominent real estate figures, including Cheng Linsheng, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Yiting, Shen Tianxin, Wei Tingrong, Gui Yanfang, and others. Cheng Linsheng presided over the meeting. It was decided to establish a Commercial Economic Association with the aim of using real estate merchants as the core group to devise measures to alleviate the economic situation. Yu Qiaqing, Cheng Linsheng, and forty-three others were appointed as chairmen, and a number of directors were designated to draft the association's charter and outline in order to register with the authorities and obtain legal basis.

Proposed Issuance of 500 Million Yuan

In addition to discussing the establishment of the Commercial Economic Association, the meeting also addressed a major proposal: the issuance of 500 million yuan in currency notes. The plan involves setting aside 60% as cash reserves and securing the remaining 40% with real estate. The government would be asked to establish a deed depository. The justification for issuing 500 million yuan in currency notes is based on the belief that Shanghai currently holds 1 billion yuan in deposits. In order to circulate these deposits, the intention is to issue currency notes backed by real estate, thereby injecting vitality into the market. The proposed term for the currency notes is five years, with an annual interest rate of five percent.

Difficulties in Raising Reserves

Regarding the above proposal, the 40% real estate guarantee is not a problem, but the cash reserve aspect is particularly challenging under current circumstances. The current stagnation in Shanghai is due to a lack of mediums of exchange. Currently, the mediums of exchange in the market, besides cash, banknotes, and government bonds, cannot have a scope as broad as actual cash and banknotes. Currently cash reserves are also generally in a depleted state. Whether this large amount of currency notes can acquire the huge amount of cash reserve, enabling a part of stagnant real estate to be circulated in the market, is the most important question.

Banking Sector's Response

Yesterday, a Shen Times reporter interviewed several important leaders in the banking sector to ask for their opinions. Most of them expressed a silent attitude. However, in their private opinion, they believed that although this proposal was not without insight, it seemed to have various practical difficulties, because the preparation of cash reserve is difficult, and even after issuance, there may still be some difficulties in the circulation of the market in the future. Under the circumstances of credit crunch, the sudden appearance of such a large amount of paper money is difficult for the market to be responsible for.

Shen Tianxin's Remarks

According to the China Eastern News Agency, the Shanghai-based newspaper, the North China Daily News, reported that fifty real estate merchants held a meeting at Cheng Linsheng's residence the afternoon before last and decided to organize the Shanghai Commercial Economic Association to prepare for the issuance of 500 million yuan in currency notes to circulate in the market. A China Eastern News Agency reporter, recognizing the magnitude of the matter, visited Mr. Shen Tianxin, the director of the association, yesterday. According to Mr. Shen, the statement about issuing 500 million yuan in currency notes is not factual because the fundamental measures have not yet been determined. As for the original name of the association, it was originally the Shanghai Commercial Economic Research Association. The association was convened at Mr. Cheng Linsheng's residence at 3 p.m. the afternoon before last, and more than 120 people attended. Cheng Linsheng was publicly elected as the temporary chairman. The economic problems of Shanghai were discussed on the spot for three hours. It was said that Shanghai is the central hub of the national finance, and it has been hit the hardest. The state of tension during last year's large closures was very rare. At the beginning of this year, factories and commerce were the first to encounter difficulties, and credit loans became a formality. The newspaper reported that the money industry was unwilling to join the five million yuan silver group in written opinions. Silver reserves are drying up, and there is a shortage of capital. The funds released are not easy to recover for a while, and the real estate goods in hand are turned to others for mortgages, and they are subject to all kinds of criticisms. Therefore, it was studied that quite a lot of real estate in Shanghai has been pledged to the silver and money industries. A way out should be opened so that there can be more capital to circulate in the market, so that all industries can turn around. The money industry said that it had suffered a lot of pain in asking for help last year, and it also suffered for others. The purpose of this association is to assist the circulation of Shanghai's commercial economy. Now the name of the association is changed to the Shanghai Commercial Economic Association, and 45 directors are elected. In three or four days, members are asked to enter the association and send what they know to the association, so that the board of directors can collect everyone's opinions and prepare a presentation to the Ministry of Finance for instructions. It must also be agreed with the silver and money industries before a fundamental problem can be established. This is for the sake of more capital, not the principle of borrowing, so that the whole city can be dredged and all industries can be turned around, so as not to become a void. In the end, it was studied that the number of real estate in the whole port is very large. If it is not completely resolved, it is very worrying. Most of the directors elected are familiar with Shanghai's commerce and have rich experience.

Ministry of Finance Issues Circular Clarifying Measures to Encourage Foreign Banks to Import Silver 129

The National Federation of Chambers of Commerce, the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and other organizations received a circular from the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating that the three measures formulated by the Ministry to encourage foreign banks to import silver have been approved and instructed to be notified to the association and to instruct the Chief Inspector of Customs to announce and implement them. In order to be more clear and avoid misunderstandings, the first item of the original measures is explained and the second item is supplemented as follows: (1) The first item of the original measures stipulates that an export tax exemption passport shall be issued for the original amount of silver or national currency. The so-called original amount refers to the amount of silver and national currency (each national currency shall be based on 23.493448 grams of pure silver) equal to the amount originally imported when re-exporting. It is not limited to the original imported silver and national currency. If re-exported in batches, this tax exemption passport may also be used, but it is limited to the amount listed in the original passport. (2) Those who hold the aforementioned tax exemption passport for export shall be exempt from the silver export tax and equalization tax levied since October 15, 1934, in addition to the 2.25% tax (national currency and Central Mint bars are also exempt from the 2.25% tax). In addition to informing the Chief Inspector of Customs to comply with the announcement, the association is hereby informed. This order.
