Free Talk

Accepting Criticism 212

— Tang Tao

Mushanokōji Saneatsu once wrote a short article called "All Works of Art," strongly urging writers to steadfastly follow their own path, all the way to a place of conviction, regardless of all the trials and tribulations. His words also carried criticism, saying:

The wishful thinking demands of critics should be ignored. They are not genuinely hoping for the author to improve. They are also human and cannot fundamentally understand other people's works...

This kind of opinion is very fashionable in the current Chinese literary and art circles, and it indeed has some influence. Since last year, whether they are writers or not, everyone has been criticizing criticism, and the only method of resistance, it is said, is precisely to "ignore it."

What is being criticized is "ignored," but there are usually a few words to say to those who are 　　. Perhaps saying, "This is a Taiwanese!" or "This belongs to such-and-such school!" and the more thorough response is, "Hey! You're pointing at your own nose."

A critic wants to criticize others, but unexpectedly points at his own nose in the mirror. Although this seems like a joke, the audience's reason will never be buried in their own laughter, because they can still know that this nose is indeed very black.

People with a firm path to walk can go ahead and walk their firm path. Although there is no perfect criticism now, there are also no absolutely absurd critics. The road is always firm. Critics, from the standpoint of bystanders, only point out the thorns and forks on that road. They will never tell you to turn back.

But now it is said that even the truth is crying in pain, because critics have condemned everything.

In practice, there are also distinctions in condemnation. Cursing that begins with "Damn it!" is certainly unacceptable, but a painful rebuke that can seize on flaws and enumerate them in detail can still be accepted.

Precisely because critics "are also human," we believe that they are able to "understand other people's works."

Mason Chen Qiu 213

— Ouyang Shan

"San Huai! -- This is the twelfth time I've encountered it, that beast! It was jumping and hopping there, and grinning at me..." Mason Chen Qiu lay on a bed composed of ambiguous gray and blue, pinching his thick throat with his hand, making a few dry monkey-like laughs. The air was trapped inside his lungs, as if being squeezed out of his ears, nose, and even eyes, causing his face to become completely flushed.

With whirlwind-like force, he threw back the quilt. All the lean bones in his body, protruding outside his tattered undershirt, barely supported his overly heavy head, which seemed on the verge of falling apart every second. He hopped around on the dirt floor, trying to shake off the cold air that immediately attacked his whole body like a wasp's stinger, continuing to exaggerate to his woman - who was squatting in the pine wood smoke in front of the small stove - and mentioning their daughter A Xi's name.

"That beast is getting closer and closer to me. Grab it and don't let go, dig its throat with your middle finger, and it will turn into a bag of silver - all the wise old folks know this! Tell A Xi to guess which character to buy, will she dare to buy another character? Of course not! She can only buy San Huai, and know that her old man still has this little bit of luck. Old hag, why are you so quiet? I had such a vivid dream last night..."

The woman, who was about fifty years old, emerged from the thick smoke like drifting clouds, mechanically answering him:

"A Xi went to buy vegetables, come wash your face. You often have dreams, A Qiu."

Then Chen Qiu grumbled and cursed his woman, recalling all her stupidity, hateful mistakes, and the bad luck she brought, and then began to search for cash in every possible place.

"Gambling on character tickets isn't anything great! Only you, this heartless old hag..."

At night, on top of the five or six-zhang-high banyan trees that could not be cut down, the north wind swirled around like sea waves, brushed against, and fought with the boundless green leaves, constantly whistling them down, and then trampling them with its icy hooves. In Chen Qiu's home, sharp, womanly shouts would pierce the grand sound waves and reach the ears of the surrounding neighbors.

So they began to speculate on the mason's anger.

"Didn't something open in the morning market today, wasn't it a monkey?"

"No, a carp."

To buy character tickets, he often argued with his daughter A Xi, a twenty-one or two-year-old girl with a large forehead, dull and dim eyes hidden beneath, who seemed even more stupid and stubborn than her mother when she spoke. She didn't believe in her father's dreams, and all the hints that all character ticket gamblers gratefully accepted, and didn't even want to talk about them at all. She just casually bought a character with all her money, and then forgot about it, as if she never had any hope for what she did.

They lived in a small wooden house made of old wooden boards and zinc iron near the foundation of the new Western-style houses that were being built on a large scale in the Youtong Yamen, close to several vegetable patches planted with lettuce and green onions. In the morning, before Chen Qiu started work, his threatening voice would burst out from inside:

"San Huai! There's no other character... you dare, if I lose, I'll break your head, you spendthrift! I dreamed of being chased by ghosts again last night - what is this if it isn't a dream omen, why would I have such a dream!"

But his daughter still answered him calmly and with some annoyance:

"Everyone has their own thoughts, anyway I don't believe you."

"Then, who do you believe?"

During the coldest days of the whole winter, Mason Chen Qiu's protruding, broad and rough forehead, eyes, nose, and mouth became more swollen and red. He walked with indignant steps, leaning his body forward, his head in a posture of wanting to examine something in detail. On the road and at the workplace, his loud voice spoke without any hesitation about things that everyone already knew... A people who live a long and tasteless life, engaged in monotonous, worthless work, cannot help but stir up some quarrels or vulgar debates to fill the emptiness of the soul, or make extremely meaningless moves to pay the price for sending away loneliness.

One sunny afternoon, Mason Chen Qiu rolled off the roof of a bungalow and fell to the ground. He suddenly ended his life like this. His fellow workers all heard him shouting loudly when he was swept up by this rapid roll:

"Grab it... grab... dig its throat - middle finger!" Such, or similar sounds. No one could point out what was meant by it.

An old water carrier, like a "poop knot" sparrow squeezed into the crowd, speculated without thinking, saying:

"He's probably drunk, right? But it's too late to vomit now."

The sun shone brightly on the completely still corpse, it lay on its side, its two feet spread out diagonally, all its fingers - on the left and right of its torso - were fastened in the loose soil, as if the deceased had tried to forcefully pull up the ground, and thus fell down himself. The blood flowing from the too large head was evaporated by the sun into a red mist, bright, beautiful, and with a moist and warm fishy smell. There were no traces of horror here, nor false weeping, everything was solemn and serious... The sun spread a golden brocade quilt over it, and the clouds added a sparse black veil. Life was still happy and great.

Resistance 214

— Lin Lin

Thousands of acres of waves,

Tens of thousands of heavy waves,

Surging forward,

Impacting the rocks of my brain,

Foam splashes everywhere.

Thousands of knives,

Tens of thousands of arrows,

Open attack and covert shooting,

I stand with the body of "Thousand-Hand Buddha" and face the battle in all directions.

Pursuit 215

— Ye Cao

The Lu River is quiet.

It is exactly fourteen or fifteen, the night sky of Heilongjiang is clear and bright. No dogs barking, no roosters crowing. The silver moon, hangs high in the distant place, quietly, people have already fallen asleep.

Due to a special event, our four brothers, in such a deep night, hid in a farmer's house. Unable to resist the attack of the spring cold, we took some dry firewood, and we lit a fire.

Silently, we warmed the fire, everyone was silent. Only using our four pairs of sensitive ears to listen, whether there was anyone knocking on the door, footsteps, or gunshots outside. Because everyone's mind was calculating: deliberating.

Sincere old folks informed us that the enemy's forces in Ang'angxi are now very weak, an hour ago, we already had two hundred and fifty brothers departing there. Ang'angxi is not far from this river bank, as far as we know, it is only two and a half hours away. If we can see the firelight before dawn, then it can be predicted that our brothers have won.

If there is no news back after three hours, we will send a large group of people again. We gently stroked the fire, so that its light would not be too large, while holding our breath and listening to the sounds outside.

The universe is quiet, there is absolutely no sound worth causing our suspicion. We four brothers, are only imagining the unfolding of this event in each other's minds.

"Thump"! It seems like something fell from the wall behind.

"The messenger shouldn't be back yet, it's not time, I'm afraid there are scouts"!

One of the brothers said this.

So, after instructing a sentence: loading bullets into the chamber, we took the guns and two of us went out. We searched around Tianjia Village for a week; the black corners of the houses, the side of the big trees, we didn't find anything. Turning back, we were still warming the fire.

Having stayed in the house for less than half an hour, there was a sound outside again, this time it was a bit louder than before. We secretly slipped out, and saw a figure swaying there outside the village, we hadn't gone far, when that guy spotted us, he ran for his life, and we chased after him in the same way.

"Brother, don't shoot, let's catch him alive"! I shouted while running.

Quickly, that guy was cut down with a bayonet by this brave brother, he didn't even shout once. It happened to cut off his throat, he ran out of breath!

When we returned, passing by the embankment of the Lu River, the water was still flowing quietly. But, we saw the firelight in the distance, our hearts were laughing.

In the faint dawn, we recognized that the person we had stabbed to death was a beggar.

"It shouldn't be! Beggars have also helped us"!

The face of the brother who had stabbed him to death immediately showed an awkward sadness.

War Notes (5) 216

— Translated by Tokunaga Sunao, translated by Ye Yin

That day, for the sake of celebration, the school was closed, and there were no classes, only the principal said a few words about the fall of Fengtian City, and the great victory of the Japanese army.

In the village temple, wine for worshiping the gods was laid out. The aunt was just as happy as if the uncle was coming back from the battlefield tomorrow.

Russian prisoners were sent over. It was said that the red-bearded Russian devils captured by the Thirteenth Regiment were all to be held in a makeshift shed in the playground, so we ran to watch with the people of the village.

The Russian devils were all big guys. Just as I had imagined, their beards were all red, and their eyes were like glass, seeming very dull. All were wearing hat-like things. Moreover, the prisoners saw the faces of us children and all murmured, smiling and walking past.

"The Russian devils are laughing!"

We felt that the Russian devils were not promising. The guns and swords had all been confiscated, and they were still smiling like this. I couldn't help but feel it was incredible.

When we went home from school, we took a detour every day to see the prisoners.

"Cowardly red beards!"

"Where did your swords go?"

We cursed at the Russian devils who were tightly imprisoned from outside the bamboo fence, or threw stones in, for about an hour.

But, the Russian devils never got angry. Their long red hair was all messed up, murmuring something, and smiling at us. The Japanese guard soldiers who were walking back and forth in front of the fence of the small house, their height, could only reach their chests.

Living Characters and Dead Characters (3) 217

— Chen Youqin

I think that teaching people to read and write should never start from oneself, and speak from one's own position. Mr. Ji Ru Cao thinks that writing the wrong character doesn't matter. In Mr. Cao's pen, there are ancient books that can be used as legal guests, knowing how to distinguish, is to distinguish into the pile of old papers, how to distinguish, is to distinguish into the homes of the ancients. It's a pity that young people will not understand the meaning, so the characters that cannot be used universally are also used, the strokes that cannot be less are less, and the strokes that cannot be more are more. As a result, people can't guess the wonderful meaning of the sentence. My two colleagues and I often hold student homework together, stunned, and guess randomly.

I remember that last year when Peking University recruited students, some applicants wrote "倡明", which of course was a mistake for 昌明. Some wrote "流學生", which of course was a mistake for 留. Professor Liu Bannong made an oil poem to mock it (see Analects Issue 26), which was of course inappropriate. Mr. Lu Xun's defense (see Zhun Feng Yue Tan Page 150) was also unnecessary. In short, characters such as "倡" and "流" are all mistakes and should be corrected.

As for the greatest reason that Mr. Cao insists on, thinking that the ancients could write other people, why can't today's young people write the wrong character? Regarding this point, I feel that the words of our colleague Mr. He Zhongying can represent me, and it is okay to copy a paragraph as follows:

He's Outline of Chinese Philology, pages 79 and 80, says:

"... The ancients used borrowing, which was also writing the wrong character, which was also not appropriate. However, it has been passed down from ancient times, and it has always been popular, and now there is no way to force people to correct it. Suppose that every character can be corrected, which is the "stem father's bug" said in the Book of Changes. Even if it is not possible, can many more wrong characters be added outside the wrong characters written by the ancients? The wrong characters written by the ancients are popular to this day, the same throughout the country, so they can still be understood. If people today add many wrong characters, and use the local pronunciation of each place to write, people in other provinces and other counties will not be able to understand them, and later the characters in the whole country will definitely be different from each other, isn't this a major obstacle?... "

Mr. He's words are not groundless, nor are they particularly fond of the ancients and dismissive of the present people. He really feels that to require the unification of characters, it is best to reduce the obstacles to circulation on the characters themselves. Writing the wrong character is the biggest obstacle to the unification of characters. Mr. He said that if many wrong characters are added, people in other provinces and other counties will not be able to understand them. I think that not only people in other provinces and other counties will not be able to understand them, I am afraid that each person will write each person's wrong character. As a result, one person has one way of writing, and two people cannot understand each other when communicating! Recently, I received a letter from a junior high school classmate. From beginning to end, it was four long sheets of paper. I don't know what he was talking about, because he used many wrong characters and mixed in some dialects. After guessing for a long time, it was still incomprehensible. I am really anxious for these poor young children!

My prejudice is that those who don't know the distinction and don't understand people, of course, should correct the writing of the wrong characters. Those who know the distinction and so-called understanders should especially prohibit the wrong characters, so as to confuse the youth's vision and hearing, and make the characters unable to unify. Those who don't understand, unintentionally writing the wrong character, can still be forgiven; as for those who are so-called understanders, if they intentionally write the wrong character to boast of their erudition, it is really unforgivable. It must be known that the ancients wrote the wrong character, sometimes due to oral transmission, it was really unavoidable. We who are born today don't need to learn it, and can't learn it. I don't know why Mr. Cao, who "advises people not to read ancient books" (Note 2), wants to bring out so many "dead characters" to replace "living characters"? (According to the examples cited by Mr. Cao, "The chrysanthemum will never need to bloom from now on" was originally a harmonic couplet, not to mention. As for the character 鞠 in "There are chrysanthemums with yellow flowers", it has already become a dead character).

(Note 1) Mr. Hu Pu'an has an article "Wrong Characters Should Not Be Written", published in the 15th issue of Min Bao. (Note 2) Mr. Cao has an article "Advise People Not to Read Ancient Books", published in Reading Life. (End)

According to yesterday's foreign dispatches, London's major rate recently narrowed to 1875, further dropping to 125. New York silver prices fell by 25. Forward silver prices in Montreal also narrowed by varying degrees, from 2.8 to 4 percent. London raw gold fell by 7.5 pence. The British pound against the U.S. dollar rose by half a point, while the U.S. dollar against the British pound rose by one point. The British pound against the French franc rose by 12 points, while the U.S. dollar against the French franc narrowed by 25. The exchange market opened in the morning with the near-term selling price of the British pound at one shilling, seven pence, and 3125, and the U.S. dollar at 34.625 yuan. Compared to the closing price last Saturday, both the British and U.S. currencies tightened by 0.0625. The Central Bank's listed exchange rate showed the British pound unchanged, while the U.S. dollar rose by 125. Customs gold units narrowed by 8 percent. Chinese merchants' sentiment weakened. During this process, there were many transactions, and banks took advantage of the low prices to buy, which helped to maintain the rates. However, when Sassoon slightly offered more currency, banks also started to supply, and the process became firmer. But at noon, prices still hovered around the same levels, and banks only engaged in some reciprocal transactions. Ultimately, Sassoon wanted to offer shillings but was unsuccessful. Securities: Supply Exceeds Demand, Bond Market Declines Slightly Across the Board 221

Yesterday, the 18th, the public bond market at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange was sluggish and lacking in spirit, failing to rally. The situation on the trading floor gradually showed signs of struggling. Many were covering shorts at low prices. Although the number of shares bought on the 4th was not large, the trend had already shifted. The sluggish market price was attributed by some to the impact of Germany's forced conscription and military discipline, while others said it was related to the slim hope of securing a large loan. However, these are superficial explanations, seemingly correct but not actually so. As the settlement period approached, many bulls were rolling over their positions, while some bears were also covering at low prices. Ultimately, supply exceeded demand. Whether the future would be characterized by a squeeze on the bulls or the bears was not yet apparent. Yesterday's trading can be described as a continuous decline. Although the decline in each trade was slight, there was no rebound from morning to dusk. Although there were one or two instances where certain bonds briefly strengthened due to a slight surge in buying interest, they soon fell again under high pressure. Sellers were primarily from the 21st, 43rd, and Northern groups, while buyers were primarily from the 4th, 32nd, 48th, and 53rd groups. If the 4th continues to cover shorts, the trend may improve. Supplement to the Shanghai News

Talks

Remedial Measures After the Abolition of the Concubine System 235

— Qiuyun

At the Legislative Yuan's regular meeting the other day, there was a major dispute when deliberating Article 9 of the Draft Enforcement Law of the Criminal Code. The article stated, "The provisions of Article 239 of the Criminal Code shall not apply to those who, before the implementation of the Criminal Code, have a cohabiting relationship with someone other than their spouse for the purpose of permanent cohabitation." Those who advocated for this article said it was a way to remedy the situation of those who had taken concubines before the new Criminal Code came into effect, so that the old concubines would not be left without support. Those who advocated for deleting the article said that it clearly protected concubinage, and since the Civil Code already provided relief, adding this article was superfluous.

Both sides seemed to have their reasons, but I agree with the latter. The principle that laws should not be retroactive is a common practice in law enforcement. Therefore, a law's effect must begin after its promulgation. Thus, even though the new Criminal Code has Article 239, it can only take effect after the new Criminal Code is promulgated. Old accounts before the new Criminal Code is promulgated are originally all not counted, which needn't be said. However, after the chairman put the case to a vote, only three people supported the deletion. Presumably, people were worried about women secretly seducing men, or that wives would jointly sue concubines, to avoid a commotion.

What I want to discuss is not this, but something else. Although the concubine system has been abolished, in reality it has not been abolished in many places. If we are trying to remedy the situation of those who took concubines before the new Criminal Code came into effect, it could open the door for people to take concubines in the future. For example, for concubines taken after the promulgation of the new Criminal Code, the date on the contract of sale could be backdated. How could the authorities investigate each case? Furthermore, the number of divorce cases is increasing daily. Although this is not entirely due to the abolition of the concubine system, the abolition of the concubine system is somewhat related to divorce cases. In the past, if a married man found someone else he liked, he would either take her as a minor concubine or a major concubine (the so-called "two big heads"). Now that the system of one husband and one wife is advocated, he must divorce his first wife before he can marry a second wife. Men can remarry after divorce without any problem, but it is difficult for women to remarry. Only women like Wei Wenxiu, who have high status and wealth, or like Ruan Lingyu, who have both beauty and talent, have a way out; otherwise, it is almost impossible.

Moreover, since the decree abolishing concubinage was promulgated, it is fine for young men to be without a wife, but it is difficult for old men to be without a wife. The poor have no way to manage, and the rich find it difficult to choose a mate. Only those with superior status, such as Xiong Fenghuang, Zhang Hairuo, and Qi Xieyuan, can attract women with vanity to serve them. The only ones who suffer are a few old men with long beards. Otherwise, who would be willing to be the spouse of a withered old man? Furthermore, those who can afford to take a concubine must be well-fed and well-clothed, and women who are willing to be concubines must be forced by the whip of life and have no other choice. They are either daughters of poor families or maids from dilapidated houses. If they do not become concubines, the rich will not want to marry them, and the poor cannot afford to marry them. Poor women have one less way out.

The abolition of the concubine system is truly humanitarian, and although it is very good, it unfortunately causes many problems. This is something that the legislators did not anticipate. This is also something that should be noted and remedied after the abolition of the concubine system.

Someone Writing in the East 236

— Xiaohong

It's already late at night. That little table clock just struck two, but I'm very excited and not tired at all. I simply forgot that it's time to sleep.

Perhaps it's the power of alcohol? At dinner, I had a drink with some friends—just one drink—and then went to a friend's house to chat for a while. By the time I got home, it was past midnight, and I'm still very excited. I've inexplicably shed tears several times.

Perhaps you'll laugh at me for being too weak. Why shed tears for no reason? Crying won't solve anything.

If you really say that, or think that way, then I want to tell you loudly: Crying is definitely not a sign of my weakness. Didn't I already say that it's for no reason? Because I don't feel sad at all. Although I know my mood isn't very good right now, it's definitely not sadness, definitely not sadness! Do you understand?

I have so much to tell you, but I don't know what to say first. Ah, my emotions are too agitated. What should I say to you first?

Yes, let me first tell you about my motive for coming to see you that day. I gave you a letter, and you didn't reply for several days (usually you reply so quickly, right?). So I recalled the contents of my letter. I thought, perhaps I offended you, misunderstood my meaning, and thought I looked down on you. But isn't it true, my friend? In our times of distress, in our times of melancholy, we should rationally encourage each other. Wouldn't saying such melancholic and sentimental words only make us more melancholic and sentimental?

However, I ultimately believed that such a thing should not cause a misunderstanding in our friendship. Therefore, I made a special trip to prepare to explain to you, or to exaggerate, to apologize to you.

But in the end, I didn't say it, because from your words, I knew that you were still the same as before and didn't misunderstand my meaning.

Lately, life has been like this. I play every day, and I also do things every day. Because life has created a stronger meaning for me. I train myself every day, and I whip myself every day, to prevent myself from falling into the swamp of decline. I try my best to find happiness, although I often can't find it and often return home with a belly full of melancholy and a belly full of sadness. But when I come home and see the work diary on my desk, my strong will raises its head again. I feel that the more ruthless society is to me, the more I should survive more strongly and harder. If someone touches a single hair on my body, I have to return a heavy punch. Moreover, in this society, those who have the same experience as you and me, or even worse than mine, are everywhere. For myself, and for those who share the same fate as me, how can I so easily become decadent and passive?

Friend, it seems that you are really becoming distant from me, as you said! But this will definitely not cause me to be pessimistic. Those who don't understand me are gradually becoming distant, which is inevitable. Just like how I treat them, because I can't understand them, we naturally walk further and further apart.

Of course, there are quite a few friends who can understand me, but what percentage is this so-called understanding? At most, they only understand some outlines of me, or even those outlines are a bit blurry.

Because of this, I can't help but feel desolate (especially in this environment where the lonely moon hangs high and all sounds are silent). So I picked up my pen to write you a letter, because I thought that you at least understand the outline of me clearly.

There have been many tragedies among my friends recently. Although I am an observer, these shadows often rise to my heart and cause me infinite nameless melancholy.

Every young person in today's society is too depressed.

It's already three thirty now. I think I should go to sleep quickly, because I still have things to do tomorrow morning. Although I'm still so excited and don't feel tired at all, I'm sure I'll have insomnia when I lie down in bed, but I have to sleep.

If possible, I would really like to have a chance to talk to you at length.

A Melancholy Woman 237

— Yafei

Because I love some seascapes, I always have to walk through that charming soft mist every morning and go to the beach, sit on a flat piece of mica stone, watching the crimson sun slowly rise from the eastern horizon, rendering the sea completely blood-red; the morning mist covering the sea gradually shrinks.

I sit alone on the stone by the sea, flipping through a novel, listening to the surging sound of the waves, carefully chewing on my lonely mood, and recalling dreamlike past events. - For two years, whether in winter or summer, I have never missed a day, unless it rains, I would be wistfully stuck in the house.

Two years like a day, every day I come here to spend a lonely morning; many books have been turned over from my hands here one by one. Two months ago, a woman suddenly appeared on this beach, estimated to be about twenty years old, her face was as pale as a piece of white paper. However, judging from her dress, she was at least a aristocratic modern young woman. Every day she always carried a leather suitcase, dragging a heavy step, stumbling along the beach, sometimes sitting on a rock by the sea, silently, silently watching a stack of waves rolling to the beach, letting the sea breeze blow her hair fluttering, as if thinking about something?

Her beauty cannot be completely covered by her haggardness, but her beauty also cannot hide her melancholy; a kind of inner sadness is often revealed in her slight sighs. She does this every day, without glancing at me, as if she doesn't feel that there is another me on this beach.

Her time seems to be earlier than mine. When I arrive at the beach at six o'clock every day, she is already wandering or sitting silently there; she always goes back after eight o'clock. One day, driven by curiosity, I waited for her to leave, so I followed her, preparing to explore the secret; but after only two turns, she seemed to know that I was specially following her, and she turned around.

Terror 238

— Made by Saobai

Page 19

She threw me a contemptuous look, which couldn't help but make me turn around and flee, as if an explorer defeated by a beast had returned home, regretting why I was so reckless; perhaps she would suspect that I had bad intentions and dare not come to this beach again tomorrow. I hardly closed my eyes all night, immersing my thoughts in curiosity and suspicion, and exploring the truth.

- How mysterious is her behavior! But why is she so depressed?

- Should she have a man? No, maybe she is already a remnant flower abandoned by the roadside!

- Her family will never be one that cannot afford meals!

- Perhaps she is a pitiful person who has exhausted the tastes of the world!

- Yes, she must be a patient with lung disease!

These questions kept swirling in my mind, but I couldn't find a proper answer.

The next day, I went to that beach as usual, but she was still there before me: and still like usual, seemed to have forgotten yesterday's affairs. On the other hand, I was a little cramped, wanting to step forward to apologize to her, but I didn't dare to be presumptuous, for fear of backfiring and causing trouble, so I finally didn't have the courage. Even though I wanted to ask her about her life several times, or I could find a way to comfort her and persuade her, but in the end, I didn't.

Now it has been more than a week since she was last seen on this beach; but I still go there every day. The beach, the waves, the tidal flats, the eastern morning sun, and the misty soft fog... everything is still so great, so beautiful, even so quiet: but where did that melancholy person go!

Mother 239

— Yonghui

My mother is already sixty years old this year! I left my lovely hometown when my mother was fifty-four years old, and now it has been a full six years since I last saw my elderly mother.

Six years of life have worn me down extraordinarily! It's as if I never had an innocent and lively childhood: I've become taciturn and rarely smile. When I see my closest friends, I only ask if they are doing well. The childish habits of shouting and jumping can no longer be found on me, although sometimes I really want to cheer up and play with a group of companions of similar age.

How long six years is! Living in the whirlpool of unemployment, I can feel it even more.

The year I left home, my mother already had gray hair: now, it's probably all white.

Letters from home always say that the countryside has suffered from floods, droughts, and wars. Whenever I receive such a pair of letters from home, my melancholic heart, which has been wounded by life and entangled by sorrow, is even more saddened by this desperate cry from home! On my existing scars, a deep line is added. Often, after a moment of stunned standing, I unconsciously fall on the bed and sob softly! The shadow of my mother flashes in my mind like lightning:

A round, anemic face, and when she speaks of something that she can't find a solution for, her eyebrows are locked in a line, her mouth is tightly closed, and her muscles twitch... This is the vague outline of my mother that I can remember.

I can now recall the embarrassment of my mother six years ago when she sent her pampered and sheltered young son to Shanghai thousands of miles away to find his brother. I know that my mother's heart was more painful than if a sharp knife had been inserted into it! Even more painful!

Since the year I left, from my mother's letters, I knew that the family was getting worse every year! In the second year, my mother didn't even have porridge to eat, so she was taken away by my second sister. Until now, she has been at my second sister's house for a full five years?

My second sister certainly doesn't have anything to say, because after all, she is her own mother! But my brother-in-law is different and often speaks badly of my mother behind her back. My mother's ears are not deaf, and soon these rumors invade her old ears?

With an unusually stubborn mind, (in ordinary times he always said that he would not rely on anyone to support him except his son!) and usually holding the principle of "not asking anyone for anything", how can my mother endure this kind of stimulation that she has never experienced in her life?

I seem to see a withered old woman, with her gray hair scattered, drowning in the sea with tears on her face, begging me for help with the most miserable cry of mankind - that is my mother - but I myself am a poor worm who can't swim, watching her pale head sink down, only a few strands of white hair rise and fall on the surface of the water before disappearing...

Amateur Mailbox

A Discussion on Several "Quickhand Characters" 240

Editor:

After the "May Fourth" Movement, people actively promoted a more accessible vernacular Chinese to replace the profound classical Chinese for the convenience of application. Now, for the convenience of writing practice, there is also the promotion of "quickhand characters". It can be seen that the development of culture is entirely due to the evolution of the times and the needs of the masses, and it is not produced by chance.

The convenience of "quickhand characters" has already been mentioned by the editor, so I don't need to say more. However, I have a question about quickhand characters that I would like to raise and ask the gentlemen who advocate this type of writing to give me an explanation.

The vocabulary of quickhand characters has already been selected by the promotion association to consist of three hundred characters, and more will be published in the future. However, among these three hundred quickhand characters, there are a few characters that are not simple enough. For example, why not write the character "馬" (horse) as "马"? Why not write the character "縣" (county) as "县"? Why not write the character "疊" (stack) as "垒"? Also, why not write the character "癮" (addiction) as "流"? I think it seems much more convenient to change the four dots of the character "馬" to a "一" (one). It is easier for masses to understand "疊" as "垒," "縣" as "县", and "癮" as "疣," and they are also quite prevalent in the habits, so why not make it simple? Therefore, I would like to raise this for everyone's discussion. Perhaps my opinion is a bit wrong? Or is there a special reason? Please give me an instruction to avoid me and other readers from being suspicious. Respectfully submitted, Yu Fangjing

Editor's Note: Mr. Yu is to be admired for his ability to study quickhand characters in such detail and to offer several opinions.

We very much agree with his opinion, because since quickhand characters aim for simplicity, then of course we should adopt simpler characters. However, there is one point that Mr. Yu needs to understand: that is, although quickhand characters take simplicity as their goal, we must also pay attention to whether they are commonly used. At the same time, quickhand characters are only being promoted, not manufactured. Like the characters "马," "垒," and "昙" that Mr. Yu mentioned, many people are already using them, so of course there is a need to adopt them, but the writing of "县" is rarely seen. I think very few people probably recognize it, right? Since it is not common, it cannot be considered a "quickhand character" for the time being.

We know that no matter what we do, there are always some oversights in the beginning, and it must be improved by many parties before it can reach perfection. If we want quickhand characters to move forward, we must also have gradual improvements. Therefore, we hope that readers will deeply explore quickhand characters, and like Mr. Yu, contribute their own opinions at any time; at the same time, we also hope that readers will write down any simplified characters that they know and that have not been included in the three hundred characters and send them to us at any time. This column will release them as needed to serve as reference and adoption for those responsible for promoting them.

Zheng Bo Invades Chen (Continued)

A ruler must think that the people's resentment cannot do anything, so he dares to be tyrannical and oppressive; he must think that financial scarcity cannot do anything, so he dares to be lewd and extravagant; he must think that his subjects cannot do anything, so he dares to reject advice; he must think that exhausting soldiers cannot do anything, so he dares to act recklessly. These "what can be done's" are where evil deeds originate. If one does not explore the root of these things, then the words "what can be done," though containing the seeds of chaos, have not yet taken shape; though possessing the reality of something to be feared, have not yet left a trace. If one is not a wise and perceptive gentleman, who can stop the waves of disaster at their very beginning? (End)

Lapses in Etiquette at Alliances and Engagements The art of observing people lies in what is hidden, not what is obvious; in what is obscure, not what is clear. The obvious and the clear are what people fear. The hidden and the obscure are what people neglect. What people fear, even petty people know to adorn themselves. What people neglect, even gentlemen cannot be without fault. One's demeanor in public must be solemn even in private moments. One's words to guests must be strict even in casual conversation, especially during alliances, engagements, or tribute ceremonies. Gold and stone are in the courtyard; food vessels are on the mat; the ushers are in front; the three bows are below. A slight change in expression in the hall can become the laughingstock of the nation. A single word mistaken can give rise to ten thousand mouths criticizing. Human nature loves to win and hates to be humiliated; cannot one force oneself to be careful for even a moment?

Shen Bao Architecture Weekly

The Cooperation Between the Construction Industry and the News Industry 245

— Ying Dai

—The Hartford Times Newspaper in the United States Holds an Architectural Exhibition—

Since its inception, this journal has collaborated with the architectural community to hold an architectural exhibition. Indeed, the evolution of the construction industry requires the cooperation of newspapers. Holding an architectural exhibition is a very common event, but for a newspaper to initiate such an exhibition is an uncommon occurrence, not only in China but also in the United States, where the construction industry is developed. Recently, the Hartford Times newspaper in Hartford, Connecticut, USA, held a large-scale architectural exhibition. The Hartford Times already had an architectural society with a three-year history. Initially, only a few small rooms were set aside in the newspaper office to display a small number of construction materials. Recently, the scope was expanded to hold a larger architectural exhibition, including materials such as wood, partitions, tiles, carpets, paints, wallpaper, oil, faucets, stoves, water heaters, roofing materials, flooring, bathroom fixtures, and more.

On the opening day, the mayor of Hartford, the Architectural Association, and construction material merchants all attended. Visitors were not limited to Hartford city residents but came from the surrounding suburbs as well. Because the newspaper had promoted the event beforehand, the number of visitors was larger than usual. On the day of the exhibition, the newspaper spared no expense in devoting significant space to publishing architectural articles and news. Furthermore, the Hartford Times has always had a special architectural section every Saturday, dedicating several pages to articles on modernizing residences, building real estate, and decorating. The Architectural Society also collaborated with experienced and capable individuals to conduct a thorough investigation, which yielded many valuable reports that could promote construction. The investigation lasted for six weeks, and the most valuable finding was that many people wanted to build houses but lacked plans, saying they were about to start planning. Others said they had the financial means to build houses, while some wanted to join the society to study architectural knowledge.

The Hartford Times realized that many people wanted to study architecture. Therefore, they moved the building models from the middle floor to the top floor, completely isolating it from the city hall. In this room, various gatherings were held, both in the evenings and afternoons. No fees were charged for joining the studies, allowing the general public to have the opportunity to study architectural science. The society also installed an electric kitchen, preparing to cook once or more per week, and offered various games. The membership reached at least 150 to 200 people. This architectural society was established in 1928, and its various activities were further developed after 1929. Looking back, the Hartford Times collected or borrowed photographs of several buildings and published photos of old houses in the newspaper, pointing out how to improve them and make them more modern. After the news spread, the first week the architectural special section was greatly expanded, many construction companies, construction material factories, and construction material retailers placed advertisements, with text occupying seven pages. Throughout 1929, the Saturday editions occupied twelve pages, sometimes increasing to sixteen pages. In addition to advertisements, there were many valuable articles and photographs. From then on, the Hartford Times has always paid extreme attention to the construction industry and architecture.

Architectural Materials Science (6) 246

— Zhu Zhenmu

(4) Then close it again, lower the furnace temperature, and take out the wrought iron.

(5) Pour out the slag and pour into molds to cut into long strips or other shapes.

Section 3: Properties and Applications of Wrought Iron (1) Because wrought iron is cut into strips, it has a fibrous structure inside, with the direction the same as the cutting direction. If wrought iron is struck on a small clay board, the sound is very dull, which is a point of difference from the sound of steel.

Wrought iron does not rust easily, so it is often used as water pipe material.

The strength of wrought iron is far less than that of steel.

The market for wrought iron is also measured in tons, and its price is more expensive than pig iron.

Chapter 4: Steel

Section 1: What is Steel

Steel is obtained by further forging pig iron that is smelted from iron ore. The principle is simply to remove and burn away the impurities contained in pig iron and add various required materials. As for steelmaking methods, there are the Open-hearth method, Bessemer method, carburizing method, crucible method, and electric furnace method, etc. These are described separately below:

Section 2: Open-Hearth Steelmaking Method

This method is a method of directly making steel from pig iron. The raw materials used, in addition to pig iron, also include scrap steel and iron ore. Therefore, there are specialized businesses that collect scrap steel and iron, which is for this purpose. The three materials are placed in the furnace and burned with intense heat. They are melted together, and the oxygen in the iron ore is automatically released to absorb the impurities in the pig iron and scrap steel, resulting in pure steel.

The steps of the process: The furnace walls must be built with alkaline bricks containing magnesium and calcium. When in use, pig iron, iron ore, and scrap steel are first piled into the furnace, and then limestone is added. Flames and air are introduced into the furnace. After seven or eight hours, sulfur and phosphorus can be removed, and the carbon content also reaches the lowest level. Then, a small amount of ferromanganese ore sand is added to maintain the carbon content, so it is not lost, and to drive away excess gas. A small door is opened to allow the molten steel to flow out and into molds to obtain steel ingots. These can be rolled into steel plates or steel strips by machines at will. The current method used by the Longhua Shanghai Steel Mill is the above method, but the output is only sufficient to supply the military and has not yet been exported to the construction industry.

The reason why alkaline materials are used for the walls is that pig iron and iron ore often contain phosphorus, which is harmful to the quality of steel and must be removed. Therefore, it is used to remove phosphorus. If the iron ore does not contain phosphorus, ordinary siliceous mud bricks can be used, which can save a lot of cost, as magnesium bricks are extremely expensive.

Section 3: Bessemer Steelmaking Method

The Bessemer method of steelmaking is different from the above method. In the above method, the impurities are removed with iron ore, while this method only uses heat to burn away the impurities contained in pig iron. After the impurities in the pig iron are burned away, an appropriate amount of carbon is added to form steel.

The steps of the process: First, put half a furnace of pig iron into the furnace. Use a pipe at the bottom of the furnace to force air in at a pressure of 20 pounds per square inch. The oxygen in the air combines with the silicon, magnesium, and other substances in the pig iron due to the high temperature, which can cause a yellow flame to appear. When the carbon in the pig iron is oxidized by further burning, the flame turns white. This indicates that it should not be burned any further, otherwise, the pig iron will also be oxidized. The supply of air is immediately stopped, and a little carbon or manganese is added to form steel.

Section 4: Carburizing Method

This is an ancient method of forging high-grade steel materials, but it is very costly. The forging does not involve mixing with other materials but only adding a carbonaceous material, hence the name carburizing method:

The steps of the process: Place wrought iron into a small box of carbon powder and heat at a temperature of 1500 to 1800 degrees Fahrenheit for several days. At that time, every 20 hours, the iron can absorb 1/6 of an inch of carbon. After it is successfully removed from the box, gradually let it cool, and it can be used.

Section 5: Crucible Steelmaking Method

The crucible steelmaking method is also one of the forging methods of high-grade steel materials and also uses closed burning, but it is a newer method than the previous method. How is it faster and better than the previous method? First, put wrought iron into a graphite crucible that has been pre-filled with a considerable amount of carbon. The crucible is sealed airtight, and the crucible can hold about 75 to 100 pounds of iron. Burn with intense heat for five hours. The iron is dissolved and mixed with carbon to form steel. It is poured from the crucible into a mold and can be used in the market.

Architectural Jargon (7) 247

— Mei Huanzhen

Hip - Assuming the roof has a slope with three sides draining water. The raised area between the two is the roof ridge. This ridge is called the Hip.

Nogging Piece - When building a wall to a certain height or length. The first thing to pay attention to is the "protection" method of the wall. A two-by-four inch pine wood is placed in the center of the wall and nailed on both ends. This is called a Nogging Piece. It is indispensable when building a five-inch wall.

Red Lead - Whether it is ironware or wood. The first coat of primer is mostly made with red lead. Because its properties can prevent ironware or wood from rusting and rotting.

Ear - Anything that protrudes. Like an Archattave, soaring at both ends of the Lintel, shaped like an animal's ears. Scissors Brace - The phase-long material between the Joist files is used to firm the Gutter itself and prevent it from shaking. This is called a scissor brace. (A flat-topped gutter is not suitable.)

Center To Center - This means the distance between the middle from one side to the other. The cut in the construction site is called Center To Center.

Outside Line - Measuring a house, such as the dimensions of the exterior wall and exterior wall, is called Outside Line. Conversely, the dimensions of the Interior Wall and the interior wall are called the In inside Line.

Deviation - When the wall is gradually built up, if the plasterer assumes it is "so-so". Then. For work, it may be withdrawn and polluted. For example, do not take lines, do not scrape buckets, do not pull seams, and so on. The important thing is not to take the line. This situation is inevitable. Because when the bricks are casually placed on the wall with ash and sand without tapping the line, the deviation can be found within the height of one zhang. Deviation means that the wall is sloping outwards, and some places are tilting inwards. This is called exempt. If a deviation is found on the wall, this crime will be blamed on the supervisor's failure to monitor and correct the problem. Therefore, the Foreman in the construction site should pay attention to it.

Load Bearing - A large material that rests on the wall and can be used to place the joists on it.

Truss - Its organization includes the Trimming Beam, the Principa wood, the King Post, the Queen Post, the Strut, the Purling, the Common Rattor, the Creeping, and other names.

Eyebrow Iron - The lower cap of a double iron door is equipped with two small turntables. This turntable can move on two curved iron rails. This rail should be called eyebrow iron in the construction site. (To be continued)

Talking about Cement 248

— Hua

The ancient Romans already knew that after grinding and mixing volcanic ash and lime, adding water and mixing, they could gradually solidify. This antique cement is still very strong and perfectly preserved in many places. The cement on the market today is actually just blast furnace slag and lime ground together. In China, because steel manufacturing has not yet been developed, we use clay to replace blast furnace slag. This manufacturing method is actually exactly the same as the Roman method.

The components of cement. Generally speaking, they are calcium oxide, aluminum trioxide, silicon dioxide, iron trioxide, magnesium oxide, etc., but they are all in a combined state. The combination of these many oxides does not give us any conclusions from chemical analysis. Therefore, this problem has been a matter of debate among scholars for fifty years since Lai Qitali Lo Chatlier. Based on the theories of various schools, we can boldly say that cement contains and a small amount of Magnesium oxide is usually no longer combined with other things. If we only manage these oxides and no longer look at their mutual combination, then the composition of cement can be expressed as follows.

Calcium oxide 63 percent

Aluminum trioxide 6.5 percent

Silicon dioxide 21.5 percent

Iron trioxide 2.5 percent

Magnesium oxide 2.5 percent

Sulfur trioxide 1.5 percent

There are two methods for manufacturing cement: the dry method and the wet method. The wet method is popular in Europe. The dry method is a relatively new method invented by the Americans. These two methods are largely the same. In the wet method, limestone and clay are mixed with water, then ground finely and baked into small pieces. In the dry method, the raw materials are first dried, then ground finely, and then baked into small pieces. The baking temperature is about 1400 to 1600 degrees Celsius. At this time, these raw materials are in a semi-molten state. Because they are baked in a rotary kiln, these semi-molten things stick together, becoming hard blocks about the size of walnuts. After cooling, these hard blocks are ground finely by machines, and you get cement. The rotary kiln used to manufacture cement is a very long and large round tube laid flat. The diameter of this round tube is about seven to nine feet, and the length is one to two hundred feet. It rotates very slowly, about once or twice every minute.

The above outlines some common knowledge about cement. Below, I am going to talk about some recent trends in cement research.

In recent years, the phenomenon of heat generation during cement solidification has attracted great attention. According to the experiments of Danwei and Fox, the temperature of huge ternary soil buildings, such as dams, dikes, and bridge piers, can rise to 50 or 70 degrees Celsius during solidification. When the temperature of this type of building gradually cools down, the cement has already solidified, but objects expand when heated and contract when cooled. Cement, which has solidified and hardened during cooling, will crack due to contraction. To avoid cracks in buildings, the heat released by cement must be reduced. According to recent tests, the amount of heat released is greatest for tricalcium aluminate, second for tricalcium silicate, and the smallest for dicalcium silicate. Therefore, the architectural community today has great hope for cement with excellent properties and low heat release.

How does cement that has solidified erode when it encounters seawater or acid solutions? This is also a major problem today.

Solutions such as sodium sulfate, potassium sulfate, magnesium sulfate, and calcium sulfate can all erode ternary soil, and the extent of erosion depends on the concentration of these sulfates and the condition of the ternary soil. Generally, calcium hydroxide in cement reacts with acid to form calcium sulfate, and hydrated calcium aluminate becomes calcium sulfoaluminate. Both of these effects can cause ternary soil to expand and disintegrate. The effect is more severe in magnesium sulfate solutions. Because of the condition, its FH value is 10.5 at this time, which is much lower than that required to maintain hydrated calcium silicate in a stable state. Therefore, hydrated silicate calcium undergoes hydrolysis, generating several calcium hydroxides. This newly formed calcium hydroxide then reacts with magnesium sulfate to produce calcium sulfate and magnesium hydroxide. The hydroxide of magnesium in the solution continues to be in a saturated state, so the hydrated acid calcium continues to hydrolyze. This process is repeated over and over again until the small pores of the ternary soil are filled with magnesium hydroxide precipitates, making the process slow down and gradually stop. The cement has been heavily eroded and gradually becomes loose.

For ternary soils that must be eroded by seawater or acids, special cement, such as alumina cement, should be selected during construction, which will be more durable.

Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special

Preliminary Proposal for Establishing the Ruan Lingyu Acting Award 249

— Xudong

The tragic death of Ruan Lingyu has caused immense sorrow to those who care about Chinese cinema. This is because Ruan Lingyu's death is a loss to the Chinese film industry. Due to her suicide, people cannot forget Ai Xia's suicide a year ago. Thus, people cannot help but say with sorrow: The suicides of film actors have become a trend. For the future growth of Chinese cinema, we must do our best to curb this undesirable trend. Furthermore, Ruan Lingyu's death cannot but have a negative impact on people. In this distressing era, it is a terrifying hint to those who are timidly struggling in distress. Then this cannot but be something that deserves our concern even more. Moreover, news of youth suicides is constantly appearing in newspapers, although this is not necessarily due to Ruan Lingyu's influence.

Because Ruan Lingyu's suicide followed Ai Xia's, people are passionately exploring the reasons for the cowardice of Chinese film actresses. I remember this publication's article "In Memory of Ms. Ruan Lingyu" pointed out the cause of her death: Due to the contradiction between the pursuit of an upward spiritual life and the pursuit of an upward material life, she could not find an appropriate solution in this contradiction. That is to say, she could not escape the pain of this contradiction. She could not bravely sacrifice personal enjoyment and dedicate herself to a great future. Thus, she cowardly committed suicide. Others have correctly pointed out that Ai Xia's death was due to her inability to move from the current stage of capitalism to a new future, while Ruan Lingyu was unable to, like Ibsen's Nora, attain the social status that one should have in this current stage from the position of a little squirrel.

Therefore, due to this tragic lesson, we should ignite the torch of indignation from the regret for the death of an artist and from the resentment of the evil forces of society, and bravely shout in the darkness to march towards a bright future. In particular, film actors should awaken from this tragedy, deeply understand reality, and more accurately understand the historically decisive future. Then, they should promote their knowledge and confidence through film art. At the same time, they should simplify, make plain, and scientific their private lives as much as possible, and devote their lives to the struggle of art. Only in this way can there be a great artistic future, only in this way can we truly learn a valuable lesson from Ruan Lingyu's tragic death and practice it bravely, and only in this way can we most meaningfully commemorate Ruan Lingyu.

Of course, we dare to say that Ruan Lingyu is worth commemorating, but it does not seem that casting a bronze statue is enough. What is needed is to go beyond formal commemoration and become a powerful encouragement for general actors in life and art. That is to say, from the change of life to the effort of acting, as the most genuine commemoration. Therefore, here is a proposal to establish the Ruan Lingyu Acting Award.

We know that there are various academic awards in foreign countries. The famous Nobel Prize is a good example, and in the United States, there is also an annual award ceremony related to film. However, in China, such an organization is still lacking. It cannot be said that people in our society do not have a deep concern for films. Now, in principle, people probably will not oppose the realization of the performing arts award, because this will help the progress of Chinese films in any case. However, now after Ruan Lingyu's death, we believe that this kind of award is more meaningful and necessary. As mentioned above, if film actors want to have great achievements in acting, they must deeply appreciate reality. At the same time, they need to minimize and even eliminate the contradictions between personal life desires and artistic activities. In other words, they should devote their entire body to artistic labor and completely dedicate themselves to the future of art. Furthermore, there must be no contradiction between life and will. An actor who truly serves the social group must cultivate a spirit of hard work and endurance in life. Immersing oneself in a decadent life or love entanglements all day long cannot lead to great achievements in art. If life and will are completely unified, if artistic exploration is elevated above the desires of life, then suicide due to personal distress will not accidentally happen. Needless to say, the glorious award should be won by those who truly strive for film art. This kind of glory and encouragement will definitely be helpful to the progress of Chinese cinema.

However, it must be earnestly stated that this kind of award is best obtained truly from society. It must be obtained from the people who care about Chinese cinema and lament Ruan Lingyu's death, so that it will have greater significance. As for how much funding to raise, and what methods to use to raise it, how to manage it, and how to select the winners, etc., we must wait for the readers—especially those engaged in the film industry—to put forward valuable opinions. This is just a preliminary proposal.

Film Review

Review of "The Man Who Reclaimed His Head" 250

— Ling He

The Man Who Reclaimed His Head

—Great Shanghai—

In order to introduce this film to the Shanghai audience, the entire story must be briefly narrated here.

The subtitles show "Paris—1915". What unfolds on the screen is the German air force raiding Paris at night. The sirens blare, the searchlights illuminate, the planes bomb, and all the lights in the city go out. In the tense atmosphere, a young protagonist in military uniform, holding his young daughter and carrying a suitcase, staggers to the door of his former classmate, now a lawyer. Upon meeting, the protagonist, with tears in his eyes, recounts his past:

This young protagonist is named Wan Lin. He is an unsuccessful writer. One year before World War I, he lived with his beloved wife and young daughter in a quiet place in Paris. On a carnival night, news mogul Tan Meng visits Wan Lin and asks him to write current affairs articles on his behalf, under Tan Meng's name. Wan Lin initially refuses, believing that this is inappropriate behavior. However, life forces him, coupled with the persuasion of his wife who desires a comfortable life, to start writing articles for Tan. Wan Lin has always advocated peace, so he publishes speeches opposing war and promoting peace. As a result, Tan Meng's name is enthusiastically supported by the people of the whole country. At this time, Wan Lin feels very comforted in spirit, in addition to having a happy life. At the same time, Wan Lin's wife also has the opportunity to go in and out of Tan Meng in the expensive social circles. The beautiful music and dance make her deeply intoxicated.

However, because the anti-war tone in the newspaper is too high, on the one hand, it makes the people excited, but at the same time, it worries the general arms dealers, because they are trying to profit from the war. So the arms dealers give Tan Meng a huge amount of money, so that he changes from being against war to advocating war. Of course, this is exactly what the despicable Tan Meng wants, originally he was making profits by commenting. Therefore, he suddenly changes his attitude and takes the opportunity to advocate war. When Wan Lin goes to question him, his reason is for the country, for the sake of loving the motherland. Precisely because Tan Meng's name has always been admired by people, his advocacy has also aroused the frenzy of the blindly following the nation to participate in the war. Wan Lin accidentally puts forward the idea of anti-war, but is beaten by the masses. At this time, Tan Meng is in a warship discussing making money with the arms dealers.

When the war breaks out, Wan Lin is drafted to the front line. Needless to say, he tastes the pain of war. At the same time, his wife and daughter at home also miss him very sadly. When the wife receives a letter from her husband, and the little daughter asks her mother to read the letter to her, the painful heaviness cannot but make people shed tears. At the train station, when Wan Lin is reading a letter from home, he suddenly hears from someone who witnessed his beloved wife and Tan Meng being intimate in the theater, talking about Tan Meng's various misdeeds, even that he could not ask for leave to go home was also Tan Meng's doing. So in anger, he flees back to Paris. It is the night of the German bombing of Paris. In the terror of the war, he returns home and happens to see Tan Meng forcibly kissing his beloved wife. So he kills him madly, cuts off his head, and takes his beloved daughter to the lawyer's house.

The story ends here. He asks the lawyer to defend him. The lawyer asks the official to arrest him, and his wife also rushes over. They cry bitterly at each other, but the lawyer promises to defend him with all his strength. In this story, it is very clear to see the most valuable points, that is, the author of the original stage play, Jean Bart, understanding of the nature of war. The instigators of World War I were precisely capitalists such as arms dealers. In order to expand and divide the colonial market, and in order to sell their arms, they needed war. At the same time, the leaders of the imperialist press could opportunistically use anti-war arguments to win the hearts of readers (although they may not have to, as they can buy the highest reputation with money, this is the true color of so-called famous scholars). However, when they establish close ties with capitalists, loving the country becomes their best excuse, and for the pure readers, under the highest reputation, when they have already gained their belief, the effect of this deception is extremely great. The explanation of this nature has established the foundation for the success of the work. In addition, the side matching of the moral baseness and life of famous scholars and the frontal depiction of the cruelty of war, further increase the effect of the play, although we also have to point out that individual heroism, using public anger and private vengeance to punish traitors, is not the right way to oppose imperialist war.

In terms of the screenwriting techniques of the film, we seem to be able to point out: There is little depiction of the various cruelties Wan Lin experienced on the battlefield, which inevitably reduces the power of stimulation. As for the narrative of the recollection method, on the one hand, it can avoid the difficulty of connecting the air of the drama after the protagonist kills, immediately followed by the various sorrows in the lawyer's home. On the other hand, the main story, the step-by-step tense air, is not lost. However, people may feel some degree of dullness, but this cannot be said to be a failure of the director Edward Ludwig. On the contrary, he seriously treated his product with the art of film. As for the acting skills of the protagonist Claude Rains, in "Crime Without Passion", he played an extremely treacherous and evil lawyer, and has already shown great brilliance. Now here, he is a completely opposite righteous and awe-inspiring youth, and is also very conscientious. His future is truly limitless.

Ernst Lubitsch Sits at Table and Devours 251

— Meng Si

—Ernst Lubitsch, who is famous for directing American-style erotic films, recently made a big joke! It turned out that he set up a gorgeous and exquisite lunch in his villa in New York, ready to invite a few friends to have a big meal; however, unfortunately; when he scolded the car to rush to be the host, he found that everything was arranged very well, but—there was not a single guest! Because he was busy with work, he forgot all about inviting guests, so that day's feast was only enjoyed by him alone.

Film Novel

The Hate of a Vanquished Country of India (Clive of India) (3) 252

— Mao De

Many of Margaret's close friends felt that this incident was absurd and funny, and advised her not to agree, but Margaret, like the person who wrote to her, was a person with a different view. She decided her own future. Clive also seemed to know Margaret deeply, and since writing the letter, he had been looking forward to her arrival in India every day. He was not worried that she would not come. What he was worried about was how to make a career before she arrived.

At this time, the British fortress of Trichinopoly had been under siege by the French army for a long time. That was where Clive and Edmund were sent to rescue, but now they were in a desperate situation. The British army fought hard for several months and could not break through the French army's heavy siege, and it seemed that they could no longer support it. On such a night of hopeless despair, Clive and Edmund stood on the fortress's city wall. The city wall was probably more than two zhang high, with a moat below, flowing with turbid mud water. It was dark on all sides, with only the flashes of artillery fire, and one could see some east, west, north, and south. Clive looked down, and suddenly crossed one foot over the city wall.

Edmund quickly grabbed him and asked in horror, "What are you doing?" Clive gritted his teeth and said, "I'm going to ask for reinforcements. What's wrong with that?" Edmund said, "You're abandoning your duty and will be shot!" Clive pushed away Edmund's hand and said, "If I don't go, we'll all be shot." As soon as he said that, his foot had already crossed over. He squatted on the city wall, as if about to jump. Edmund shouted: "It's more than two zhang high, how can you jump?" Clive held onto the city wall with both hands, and his two feet were already suspended in the air. Edmund said anxiously, "How to report to the commander?" In a glimpse of the artillery fire, Edmund saw Clive's habitual smirk. He said, "Tell him to persevere to the end and wait for me to come back." After he finished speaking, his body was already down. .

In the council hall of Fort St. David, Governor Pigot was holding an emergency meeting. A group of East India Trading Company tycoons, Manning, Warburton, Pemberton, and Cundall, were all looking at each other, at a loss what to do. Then everyone looked around, each unwilling to look at the other, expressing the despair and the misery of doom. Captain Clarke sent in a recent report, saying that the British army was already in an urn, and there were only one hundred and twenty men left under his command. The general trend was irreversible. ,

Suddenly, a filthy and ragged man rushed in. His broken leather boots, with every step he took, the mud inside would oozed out. The military uniform on his body was already full of holes, revealing the muddy and dirty flesh inside. Everyone looked at it and opened their mouths in horror. Manning was the first to shout, "Clive, what are you doing here?" The man did not say a word, grabbed a chair, sat down, and began to poke at the broken clothes on his body. Pemberton shouted angrily, "What are you doing? This is not your bedroom!" Clive had already taken off the shirt on his upper body and wiped the mud and sweat from his shoulders. He said slowly, "Need is anyone's bedroom."

He turned his head and said to Captain Clarke, "Get some clean clothes." He also saw that there was some drink left in the large bowl on the table, so he poured it into a cup and drank it like a cow. After he finished drinking the water, he said to everyone, "Gentlemen, you have no army. Trichinopoly will soon be lost! And you! You will be looted first. Finally, gentlemen, it will be a massacre, a slaughter!" Everyone listened, looking at him listlessly. What was this news? But Governor Pigot asked kindly, "Then what is your suggestion?" (To be continued)
